### [75] [LLM-as-a-Discriminator: When Synthetic Tables Still Look Real](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09865)
*Manel Slokom,Malek Slokom,Thierno Kante*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种利用大语言模型（LLM）作为判别器，通过识别数据是“真实”还是“合成”来对表格数据进行隐私审计的方法，并验证了不同LLM模型在审计任务中的性能差异与实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在隐私保护与数据共享的矛盾中，合成数据被广泛使用。然而，针对表格数据的隐私审计目前依然困难。现有的方法往往难以准确判断数据的真实性，且人类在区分真实与合成数据方面存在局限性，因此需要一种更高效、更智能的自动化隐私审计手段。

Method: 研究提出了一种基于大语言模型（LLM）的判别方法，即要求LLM将表格样本分类为“真实（REAL）”或“合成（SYNTHETIC）”。实验在两个场景下进行：C1（仅提供表格数据）和C2（提供表格数据及分布元数据）。使用了LLaMA（开源模型）和Gemini（闭源模型）作为判别器，并在UCI Adult和ACS Census数据集上测试了CTGAN、TVAE和Gaussian Copula三种合成模型。此外，还与C2ST（分类器双样本检验）、记录链接及人工评估进行了对比。

Result: 实验结果显示不同模型间的性能存在明显差异。在Adult数据集上，LLaMA的判别召回率（DRS）为0%，而Gemini在CTGAN和TVAE模型下达到了100%。在Census数据集上，LLaMA倾向于将大多数样本判定为合成数据，而Gemini在C2设置下对特定模型表现出判别性能下降。LLM判别方法在特定条件下可作为有效的隐私审计信号。

Conclusion: 基于大模型的判别方法是一种实用的隐私审计手段。研究表明，该方法的有效性高度依赖于所选的大模型（如LLaMA与Gemini表现差异显著）、数据编码方式以及是否包含分布元数据。研究强调在进行隐私评估时，必须谨慎处理模型选择和报告机制，以确保审计结果的可靠性。

Abstract: Privacy and data sharing are often in tension. Many organizations use synthetic data to reduce privacy risk and still share useful data. For tabular data, auditing privacy remains hard. In many cases, even humans cannot easily tell if a table is real or synthetic. In this paper, we propose a method based on LLM discrimination. We ask an LLM to classify each table sample as REAL or SYNTHETIC. We test two settings: C1 with table only, and C2 with table plus distributional metadata. We use LLaMA as an open model and Gemini as a reference model. In our experiments, we run three synthesis models, CTGAN, TVAE, and Gaussian Copula, on two public datasets, UCI Adult and ACS Census. We collect 451 valid trials. Our results show clear differences between models. On Adult, LLaMA reaches DRS=0% in reported cells, while Gemini reaches DRS=100% for CTGAN and TVAE. On Census, LLaMA predicts SYNTHETIC for most samples, while Gemini stays high in C1 but drops for CTGAN and TVAE in C2. We also compare with a classifier two-sample test (C2ST) and record linkage as distributional baselines, and with a human pilot of 2 annotators and 240 trials. Our results show that LLM discrimination is a practical privacy audit signal when model choice, per provider reporting, and data encoding are handled with care. For reproducibility, code and experiment scripts are available at https://github.com/SlokomManel/LLM-as-a-Discriminator.

</details>


### [76] [Two to Tango: Coupled Task-Reference Selection for Safe LLM Fine-tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09866)
*Xinrui Chen,Jianhao Zhang,Ou Wu,Di Gao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 为了解决 LLM 在微调过程中安全性下降的问题，DualSelect 框架通过联合筛选任务样本和动态调整安全参考数据，实现了模型性能与安全性的双赢。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在针对特定任务进行微调（Fine-tuning）时，往往会牺牲预训练阶段习得的安全对齐能力。现有的方法多采用固定安全样本或简单的过滤，无法适应任务更新带来的动态安全需求，因此需要一种能同时平衡任务表现与安全性的优化机制。

Method: 提出名为“DualSelect”的耦合框架：1. 采用最小最大化（minimax）视角，在微调过程中联合筛选任务样本和安全参考集；2. 利用熵正则化评分替代指标、惰性参考刷新（lazy reference refresh）和梯度校正技术，确保任务更新不会削弱模型的安全性。

Result: 在 1B 至 8B 参数规模的 LLM 上进行了验证，DualSelect 在保持任务性能的同时显著提升了安全性。使用 REDORCA 评测显示，其安全平均分（Safety Avg.）比最强基线高出至少 5.10 分，并在多种评测指标下保持领先，且计算开销适中。

Conclusion: DualSelect 提出了一种通过同时优化任务样本选择和安全参考数据来保持 LLM 安全性的新方法，成功平衡了模型微调中的任务性能与安全对齐，并在多个基准测试中展现了优于现有方法的性能。

Abstract: Fine-tuning safety aligned large language models (LLMs) on downstream data improves adaptation but may erode learned safety behavior. Existing methods use fixed safety examples, global constraints, or one-sided task filtering. Our diagnostics show task updates expose different safety constraints, motivating joint selection of relevant references and compatible task samples. We propose DualSelect, a coupled framework for task and reference selection that refreshes task conditioned safety references before filtering whole task samples compatible with the induced reference direction. Under a minimax view, DualSelect selects safety references with high preservation loss and task conflict, together with compatible task samples, through entropy-regularized scoring surrogates, lazy reference refresh, and gradient correction. On 1B-8B LLMs, DualSelect preserves safety without losing task utility; using the REDORCA judge, it improves Safety Avg. over the strongest baseline by at least 5.10 points and remains highest in Safety Avg. across judges with moderate overhead. This view extends to retention focused continual learning.

### [77] [SPACE: Source-free Proxy Anchor Concept Erasure for MLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09868)
*Zhijing Zhang,Jiaqi Ding,Qianshan Wei,Nan Zhou,Jiaqi Li,Yongliang Wu,Tongxin Zhu,Xiaolin Fang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对多模态大模型在无法获取原始敏感数据时的遗忘难题，研究者提出了 SPACE 框架。该方法通过文本引导的代理锚点和特征空间约束，在无需目标数据的前提下实现了精准的概念擦除，且保证了模型其余知识的完整性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）面临隐私风险和监管压力，但现有的机器遗忘（Machine Unlearning, MU）方法通常依赖于目标概念的视觉数据，而这些数据由于合规限制往往无法获取。因此，需要开发一种无需原始数据的无源（Source-free）遗忘方法来删除敏感信息。

Method: 提出了 SPACE（Source-free Proxy Anchor Concept Erasure）框架，包含两个阶段：
1. 文本引导代理锚点选择（TPAS）：在共享特征空间中检索与目标概念语义对齐的代理锚点。
2. 双重约束语义隔离（DCSI）：优化这些代理锚点以间接擦除目标概念，并通过将参数更新限制在保留知识的零空间（null space）中，确保模型结构完整性。该方法通过理论证明了在保留知识不受干扰的同时最大化特征谱熵。

Result: 在六个数据集上的广泛实验表明，SPACE 的表现与当前最先进的依赖数据的遗忘方法相当。理论分析与实验结果共同验证了其在无源场景下删除敏感概念并维持模型性能的有效性。

Conclusion: SPACE 提供了一种高效、无源（Source-free）的 MLLM 机器遗忘方案。通过利用文本引导的锚点选择和双重约束语义隔离机制，该框架能够在无需原始敏感数据的情况下，成功实现特定概念的删除，同时最大限度地保留模型的通用性能，为多模态模型在隐私合规场景下的应用提供了有力支持。

Abstract: As Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) face growing privacy risks and regulatory constraints, machine unlearning (MU) has emerged as a crucial solution for removing sensitive data while preserving model performance. However, existing MU methods typically rely on visual data of the target concepts, which is often unavailable due to strict data retention policies, thus creating a demand for source-free unlearning approaches that operate without access to the target data. In this work, we propose Source-free Proxy Anchor Concept Erasure (SPACE), the first source-free unlearning framework specialized for MLLMs. SPACE consists of two stages: (1) Text-Guided Proxy Anchor Selection (TPAS), which retrieves semantically aligned proxy anchors from the shared feature space. (2) Dual-Constraint Semantic Isolation (DCSI), which optimizes these anchors to indirectly erase target concepts. DCSI confines updates to the null space of retained knowledge, ensuring structural integrity. We theoretically prove that SPACE strictly bounds the perturbation on retained knowledge and maximizes feature spectral entropy, thereby maintaining the model's performance. Furthermore, extensive experiments across six datasets show that SPACE achieves performance comparable to that of state-of-the-art data-dependent methods, validating its effectiveness in source-free MU scenarios. The source code will be released.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在联邦学习（FL）与拆分学习（SL）结合的环境中，客户端硬件能力异构导致固定切分点无法兼顾计算效率与训练稳定性，亟需一种能够动态适应资源变化的切分策略。

Method: 提出了一种基于深度 Q 网络（DQN）的框架 QSplitFL：1. 使用轻量级硬件指标（CPU、内存、电量、网络延迟）作为状态表示；2. 引入衰减式损失下降奖励函数以加速收敛；3. 采用委员会投票机制的 DQN 架构以防止奖励欺骗。

Result: 在 MNIST、CIFAR 等多个数据集及多种神经网络架构上的实验表明，QSplitFL 在收敛速度、模型准确性及资源适应性方面均优于现有的拆分策略。

Conclusion: QSplitFL 通过感知客户端异构硬件能力并动态调整切分点，有效解决了 SFL 架构中的资源瓶颈问题，在保持隐私性的同时实现了更好的模型收敛性和准确性。

Abstract: Federated Learning (FL) combined with Split Learning (SL) is a privacy preserving paradigm that enables training deep neural networks (DNNs) on resource constrained devices while reducing overall training cost. However, determining the optimal split point, meaning the layer where the model is divided still remains a critical challenge, especially when clients have heterogeneous hardware capabilities. Fixed split points can overload weak devices and increase the communication and server load, which slows convergence and reduces stability. This paper introduces QSplitFL, a novel capability-aware Deep Q-Network (DQN) framework for optimal split point selection in Split learning based Federated Learning (SFL) environments. Unlike existing approaches that rely on high-dimensional model weight representations, QSplitFL employs a lightweight state representation derived directly from client hardware metrics, including CPU utilization, memory, battery level, and network latency. The proposed framework incorporates a decayed loss-drop reward function that prioritizes early convergence, and a committee-based DQN architecture with majority voting to mitigate reward hacking. Extensive experiments on MNIST, Fashion-MNIST, CIFAR-10, and CIFAR-100 datasets using CNN, ResNet50, MobileNetV4, and ConvNeXt architectures demonstrate that our approach achieves better convergence and higher accuracy compared to existing methods, while effectively adapting to heterogeneous device resources. The source code is publicly available at https://github.com/AIPO-Lab/QSplitFL.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种名为PatchSTG的基于分块的时空图Transformer模型。该方法的核心在于：1) 利用地理信息将传感器划分为平衡且具有局部保持性的分块；2) 设计了双重注意力编码器，交替执行块内注意力（捕捉局部交互）和块间注意力（建模全局依赖），将计算复杂度从二次方降低至接近线性。

Result: 在罗德岛等多个真实交通数据集上的实验结果表明，PatchSTG在多个预测时间跨度上均实现了稳定且具有竞争力的预测性能，同时显著降低了计算开销，在大规模数据集上展现了良好的扩展性。

Abstract: Traffic forecasting is a fundamental component of intelligent transportation systems, yet remains challenging in real-world settings due to irregular sensor distributions and the high computational cost of modeling large-scale spatiotemporal dependencies. In practical traffic networks, sensors are unevenly distributed across regions, leading to non-uniform spatial structures that limit the effectiveness and scalability of existing graph-based and attention-based models. To address these challenges, we propose PatchSTG, a patch-based spatiotemporal graph Transformer designed for efficient forecasting on irregular sensor networks. The key idea is to introduce a hierarchical spatial representation that partitions sensors into balanced, locality-preserving patches based on geographic information. On top of this structure, a dual attention encoder alternates between intra-patch attention for capturing local interactions and inter-patch attention for modeling global dependencies, reducing computational complexity from quadratic to near-linear scaling. We evaluate PatchSTG on real-world traffic data from Rhode Island and additional large-scale datasets. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed model achieves stable and competitive forecasting performance across multiple horizons, while significantly improving computational efficiency. Ablation studies further validate the effectiveness of spatial partitioning and dual attention in capturing both local and long-range traffic dynamics. These results suggest that patch-based spatiotemporal modeling provides a scalable and effective framework for traffic forecasting under irregular spatial settings.

### [80] [Rotate2Think: Geometric Priming via Orthogonal Rotation to Improve Language Model Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09873)
*Aditya Sharma,Christopher J. Pal,Amal Zouaq*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过分析推理模型内部的表征空间，发现“思考”向量与“输入”向量存在独特的几何旋转关系，并据此提出 Rotate2Think 方法，通过在推理时注入几何引导向量，显著提升了模型在各类复杂任务中的推理准确率，且无需重新训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的推理模型通过生成思维链进行复杂任务推理，但内部表示空间中“思考”过程与“输入”表征的区别尚不明确，且这种空间结构能否被利用以进一步提升推理能力仍是未解之谜。

Method: 研究发现模型输入向量与思考向量呈现高度锥度（conicity）且方向不同。作者提出 Rotate2Think 方法，将从输入到思考的转换建模为旋转问题，利用正交普鲁斯特分析（Orthogonal Procrustes analysis）从少量样本中计算旋转矩阵，并在推理时将合成的思维向量注入模型，引导模型进入正确的推理空间。

Result: Rotate2Think 方法在 32 个模型与基准配置中的 30 个取得了性能提升，涵盖数学、科学和编程任务，并实现了在多模态推理任务上的零样本迁移。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了推理模型在“思考”过程中的表征具有独特的几何结构，并通过 Rotate2Think 方法证明，利用这种空间几何特性无需额外训练即可有效提升推理模型的性能，为理解和优化大模型的思维过程提供了新路径。

Abstract: Reasoning models achieve strong performance on challenging tasks by generating explicit intermediate reasoning traces before producing a final answer. Yet the internal structure of representation space when reasoning remains poorly understood: how do a model's hidden representations differ during thinking versus the embeddings of the input prompt, and can this structure be exploited to elicit stronger reasoning at inference time? We show that both input embeddings and thinking embeddings (mean-pooled last-layer hidden states over the prompt and reasoning trace, respectively) exhibit extremely high conicity, with all vectors clustering tightly around a single mean direction. Crucially, these mean input and thinking directions are non-collinear, with thinking embeddings occupying a geometrically distinct region of embedding space across many different models and benchmark tasks. This observation motivates casting the input-to-thinking transition as a rotation problem admitting a closed-form solution via orthogonal Procrustes analysis. We propose Rotate2Think, a training-free method that estimates this rotation from a small set of correctly solved examples and injects the resulting synthetic thinking vector between thinking delimiters at inference time, providing a geometric primer at the onset of the reasoning trace. Evaluated across multiple benchmarks and model families, Rotate2Think improves accuracy in 30 of 32 model-benchmark configurations across mathematics, science, and code tasks, and generalizes zero-shot to multimodal reasoning on MATH-Vision.

### [81] [Disjoint or Overlapping? Inference Windowing for Reconstruction-Based Time Series Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09874)
*Guillaume Coulaud,Reza Akbarinia,Florent Masseglia*

Main category: cs.LG

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文在TSB-AD和UCR基准上，对包括PCA、DLinear、自动编码器（AutoEncoder）、TimesNet及Transformer在内的多种重构模型进行了系统评估。通过引入统一的训练、调参及多随机种子评估协议，重点研究了推理过程中滑动窗口的重叠步长（overlapping inference）对检测性能的影响。

Conclusion: 重构类异常检测方法的性能不仅取决于模型架构与训练，推理时的滑动窗口步长（inference stride）也是决定性因素。研究证明重构类基准方法在单变量时间序列异常检测中极具竞争力和实用价值，并强调了建立统一且可重复的评估协议的重要性。

Abstract: Reconstruction-based methods are widely used for time series anomaly detection, where models are trained to reconstruct subsequences, and anomalies are identified through reconstruction errors. However, reported results are often hard to compare due to heterogeneous evaluation practices and underspecified inference procedures. In this paper, we revisit reconstruction-based anomaly detection in the univariate offline setting and study the role of the inference stride, which controls whether subsequences are processed as disjoint windows or with overlap. We propose a unified training, tuning, and multi-seed evaluation protocol on the curated TSB-AD benchmark, and study how overlapping inference affects anomaly detection performance for a range of reconstruction models, including PCA-based baselines, DLinear, an AutoEncoder, TimesNet, and Transformer variants. The results show that across all models, overlapping windows yield consistent improvements, with average relative gain up to +28%, and can alter method rankings. We further analyze variability across datasets, random seeds, and hyperparameter configurations. Finally, we complement the benchmark study with an evaluation on the full UCR archive using localization criteria aligned with sliding-window reconstruction. Overall, our results highlight that reconstruction-based anomaly detection performance depends not only on model architecture and training, but also on inference choices, motivating a clear and reproducible protocol. Our results show that reconstructionbased baselines achieve strong performance on both TSB-AD and UCR benchmarks, supporting them as competitive and practical approaches for univariate time series anomaly detection.

### [82] [Representation Curriculum: Stagewise Training for Robust Ranking and Allocation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09891)
*Ehsan Ebrahimzadeh,Sina Baharlouei,Abraham Bagherjeiran*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对数字市场中排序系统过度依赖历史偏差信号而忽略产品本质优劣的问题，本文提出“表示课程”（RC）训练策略，通过分阶段引入特征，引导模型学习更具泛化能力的内容特征，从而有效缓解冷启动困难并提升系统整体鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数字市场中，现有的排序系统过度依赖受曝光影响的反馈信号（如点击率、历史流行度），这些信号在平稳需求下预测准确，但会形成“学习捷径”。这导致模型倾向于固化现有头部商品，抑制新商品的发现，并降低模型在冷启动和分布偏移环境下的泛化能力与鲁棒性。

Method: 论文提出了一种名为“表示课程”（Representation Curriculum, RC）的训练干预机制。该方法通过在训练过程中分阶段引入特征：初期优先使用基于内容的“优点信号”（merit signals），随后逐步引入依赖于曝光的“信念信号”（belief signals），并对内容路径进行锚定约束。这种方法通过阻止模型对历史偏差的走捷径式学习，缓解了内容特征的梯度饥饿问题。

Result: 在理论上，通过高斯线性岭回归模型推导得出，RC 在冷启动目标分布下严格降低了总体风险，并量化了其与源数据性能之间的帕累托权衡。在公开基准数据集和大规模电商搜索系统的在线实验中，RC 显著提升了模型对内容特征的依赖度，在提升冷启动商品表现的同时，保持了头部商品性能的平稳可控。

Conclusion: “表示课程”（Representation Curriculum, RC）通过训练时的阶段性干预，成功解决了推荐系统对历史偏差信号的过度依赖问题。该方法不仅在理论上证明了其能有效降低冷启动分布下的预测风险，且在工业界大规模电商场景中验证了其在提升系统公平性与鲁棒性方面的实用价值，为解决数字市场中“赢家通吃”及冷启动难题提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Ranking in digital marketplaces is a dynamic exposure-allocation mechanism: displayed items shape discovery trajectories and success events logged by the platform to update future allocation policies. Modern ranking systems rely heavily on exposure-confounded signals (e.g. popularity estimates, CTR/CVR aggregates, and ID-based representation), because they are highly predictive under stationary demand. Yet this predictive power can become a learning shortcut: early access to exposure-dependent belief signals steers optimization toward over-reliance on them and away from exposure-independent merit signals (e.g., content-based competitiveness and semantic affinity). Consequently, the learned policy tends to entrench incumbents and degrade cold-start generalization and robustness under distribution shift. We propose Representation Curriculum (RC), a training-time intervention that temporally stages feature utilization. RC foregrounds content-based merit signals initially, then introduces exposure-dependent belief signals while anchoring the content pathway near the learned merit representation, curbing shortcut reliance on historical signals and mitigating gradient starvation on content signals. We formalize RC independently of task and hypothesis class and provide ranking-specific instantiations. In a Gaussian linear ridge setting, we derive closed-form solutions and sufficient conditions under which RC strictly reduces population risk on a cold-start target distribution, with a quantified Pareto tradeoff against source performance. Experiments on public learning-to-rank and recommendation benchmarks, and randomized online experiments in a large-scale e-commerce search system, show that RC measurably shifts reliance from historical belief signals toward content-based merit signals and yields consistent gains on cold populations with a controlled trade-off in head performance.

</details>


### [83] [Integrating Local and Global Entropy for Uncertainty Quantification in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09875)
*Johanne Medina,Tianyi Zhou,Keivin Isufaj,Aristides Gionis,Sanjay Chawla*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为GLU的无监督方法，通过融合大模型中间层的全局几何复杂度与局部Token级熵，显著提升了对大模型幻觉和错误预测的不确定性量化能力，有效解决了现有方法难以识别“自信但错误”的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大模型不确定性量化方法大多仅关注Token级信号，忽略了中间层隐藏状态的几何结构信息，导致模型在面对“自信但错误”的幻觉问题时表现不佳，因此需要引入全局几何特征来弥补这一缺陷。

Method: 研究人员提出了一种名为“全局-局部不确定性（GLU）”的方法。该方法将隐层状态矩阵的几何熵作为“全局不确定性”指标，与传统的“局部不确定性”（Token级熵）相结合，并通过乘法门控机制将两者融合。该方案无需训练，仅需单次前向传播即可计算，且对模型架构具有通用性。

Result: 实验表明，全局几何特征与局部Token熵在统计上近乎正交，能捕捉不同类型的失效模式。在三个模型系列和六个基准测试中，GLU方法在保持高效（单次前向计算）和长度归一化的同时，性能达到或超越了现有的所有无监督基准方法。

Conclusion: 本研究表明，将模型隐层状态的几何复杂度（全局不确定性）与Token级熵（局部不确定性）相结合，能够显著提升大模型不确定性量化的准确性，特别是在捕捉“自信但错误”的失效模式方面表现出色。GLU提供了一种高效、无监督且通用的不确定性评估方案。

Abstract: Large language models hallucinate confidently, making uncertainty quantification (UQ) essential for reliable deployment. Existing methods rely predominantly on token-level signals, leaving the geometric structure of intermediate hidden states underused. In this paper, we take the geometric complexity of hidden-state matrices as a measure of the global uncertainty of LLMs, while treating token-level uncertainty estimation as a local metric. We show that hidden-state geometric entropy (global uncertainty) and token-level entropy (local uncertainty) are statistically near-orthogonal, capturing distinct failure regimes for reliability prediction. In particular, global geometry recovers the confident-but-wrong failure mode that local signals systematically miss. Building on this, we propose Global-Local Uncertainty (GLU), an unsupervised, single-pass score that fuses the two signals via a multiplicative gate. Across three model families and six benchmarks, GLU matches or outperforms all unsupervised baselines while requiring only a single forward pass and remaining length-normalized and architecture-agnostic.

</details>


### [84] [Calibrating Overconfidence Without Sacrificing Confidence: Probe-Conditioned Head Intervention for LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09876)
*Ke Li,Chongzhe Zhang,Zifan Zeng,Feng Liu,Qunli Zhang,Zheng Hu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为PCHI的推理时干预方法，通过探针技术选择性地识别并抑制大模型的错误高置信度回答，在显著降低过拟合的同时，有效保护了模型对正确回答的自信。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型往往对错误的回答表现出过高的自信。传统的校准方法通常是全局性的或基于得分层面的，在降低不当自信的同时，往往会误伤正确回答所应有的自信心。因此，需要一种能够选择性地抑制错误高置信度，同时不损害正确回答置信度的方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为“探针条件化注意力头干预”（Probe-Conditioned Head Intervention, PCHI）的推理时方法。该方法利用冻结的探针（probe）识别出模型可能出现“高置信度但错误”的回答，并根据探针输出，有条件地重新缩放模型在生成置信度时的下游注意力头输出。通过干预读出（readout）标记或上游置信度模板标记，实现对错误置信度的选择性抑制。

Result: 在Qwen3-4B-Instruct模型上，PCHI方法成功将82.2%的错误置信度标注修正为“否”；通过联合干预，预期校准误差（ECE）从21.9%大幅降至9.2%，且仅误伤了5.1%的正确回答。该方法在Gemma3-4B上也表现出了一定的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文证明了通过条件化的内部干预（PCHI），可以在很大程度上实现对大模型“自信但错误”回答的抑制，同时最大限度地保留其对正确回答的自信，从而在抑制盲目自信与保留合理自信之间实现了较好的解耦。

Abstract: Large language models often express high confidence in answers that are wrong. Standard calibration remedies typically act globally or at the score level, reducing unwarranted confidence but also risking erosion of warranted confidence on correct answers. We introduce Probe-Conditioned Head Intervention (PCHI), an inference-time method that uses a frozen probe to detect likely wrong-but-confident responses and conditionally rescales downstream attention-head outputs during confidence generation. On Qwen3-4B-Instruct solving OpenMathInstruct problems with a structured binary confidence field, readout-token PCHI converts 82.2% of originally wrong-yes confidence readouts to $\texttt{no}$, while a joint intervention across upstream confidence-template tokens reduces ECE from 21.9% to 9.2% and damages only 5.1% of originally correct-yes readouts. The readout-token effect also appears on Gemma3-4B, though upstream interventions are weaker and more mask-dependent. These results show that verbalized overconfidence can be selectively reduced through conditionally applied internal intervention, partially decoupling the suppression of unwarranted confidence from the loss of warranted confidence.

### [85] [Streaming Knowledge Compilation: Proactive Materiality-Scored Pinning for Time-Evolving LLM Wikis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09877)
*Juan M. Huerta*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种流式知识编译框架，通过引入实质性信号预测重要文档，实现对动态知识流的高效缓存更新，并证明了以累积遗憾作为评估指标比传统的问答评分更可靠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM知识编译方法通常基于静态语料，无法处理现实中不断演变的知识流。本研究旨在解决如何在有限的Token预算下，从动态知识流中持续维护一个与离线预知最优策略遗憾最小化的编译知识库。

Method: 提出了流式知识编译（Streaming Knowledge Compilation）框架，引入实质性信号（materiality signal）作为查询相关性的代理，用于在查询到来前主动预填充KV缓存；并通过理论证明了其在 $O(\sqrt{T\log K})$ 遗憾界下的性能表现。在金融领域利用异常股价波动作为信号，在维基百科领域利用异常编辑率（AER）作为信号，并采用累积遗憾作为评估指标。

Result: 实验表明该算法在金融（累计遗憾收敛至-20.0）和维基百科（累计遗憾收敛至+16.0）领域均表现良好。证明了在资源有限的情况下，基于实质性信号的动态管理能显著优于静态缓存，并指出QA评测中存在“LLM作为裁判”对后验知识的混淆效应。

Conclusion: 研究确立了“流式知识编译”框架的有效性，证明了利用可预测的实质性信号进行主动缓存更新，能有效应对知识库的动态演变，且累积遗憾（Regret）分析比单一的问答（QA）得分更能可靠地评估知识编译系统的性能。

Abstract: LLM wiki systems compile knowledge into pre-filled KV caches for efficient inference, but assume a static corpus -- an assumption that fails whenever the underlying information landscape evolves. We formalize Streaming Knowledge Compilation: given a document stream, a fixed token budget, and future queries unknown at ingestion time, maintain a compiled wiki that minimizes cumulative regret against an offline oracle with perfect foresight. The enabling insight is a materiality signal $φ_t(k,n)\in[0,1]$ that scores document importance for entity $k$ at time $t$, acting as a query-relevance surrogate for proactive pinning before queries arrive; we prove an $O(\sqrt{T\log K})$ regret bound where $\varepsilon=\mathbb{E}[|φ_t-\hatφ_t|]$ is the only domain-specific quantity. We instantiate in two domains: finance, where $φ_t$ is abnormal stock volatility predicted by frozen Llama 3.1 8B classification head (AUROC = 0.728 on 76K articles, strict temporal split; $1.49\times$ higher realized forward volatility for predicted-material articles); and Wikipedia, where $φ_t$ is the Abnormal Edit Ratio (AER), a cross-sectionally normalized edit velocity -- showing the same algorithm generalizes beyond the finance domain. End-to-end QA evaluation on 173 matched pairs (finance) and 119 (Wikipedia) reveals a pervasive LLM-as-judge confound on post-training knowledge, establishing that regret analysis -- not absolute QA scores -- is the reliable evaluation metric for compiled knowledge systems. Finance cumulative regret converges to -20.0 (-0.12/step); Wikipedia to +16.0 (+0.13/step), with the positive sign confirming that Wikipedia edit content is genuinely post-training -- richer context consistently improves scores (No Wiki 3.80 vs. Oracle 4.74) -- and eliminates this confound. The $O(\sqrt{T\log K})$ guarantee applies to any domain where knowledge gaps can be predicted from streaming signals.

</details>


### [86] [Flash-GMM: A Memory-Efficient Kernel for Scalable Soft Clustering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10896)
*Gal Bloch,Ariel Gera,Matan Orbach,Ohad Eytan,Assaf Toledo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Flash-GMM 提出了一种基于 Triton 的高性能计算内核，通过消除冗余的显存占用，实现了 GMM 计算的 20 倍加速，并显著提升了大规模近似最近邻搜索的效率与精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的高斯混合模型（GMM）在大规模数据集上计算效率低下且显存占用极高，限制了其在处理大规模数据时的应用。

Method: 提出了一种基于 Triton 的融合内核（Fused Kernel），通过在单次 GPU 传递中完成计算，彻底消除了在显存中物化完整责任矩阵（responsibility matrix）的必要。

Result: 相比现有实现，Flash-GMM 实现了 20 倍的加速，支持训练的数据集规模扩大了 100 倍以上；在近似最近邻搜索应用中，以更低的计算成本实现了更高的召回率。

Conclusion: Flash-GMM 证明了通过融合算子技术可以高效处理大规模高斯混合模型（GMM）计算，使得 GMM 成为大规模近似最近邻搜索中比 K-Means 更优且可行的选择。

Abstract: We present \textbf{Flash-GMM}, a fused Triton kernel for efficient computation of Gaussian Mixture Models (GMMs) over large-scale data in a single GPU pass. By eliminating the need to materialize the full responsibility matrix in GPU memory, Flash-GMM achieves a \textbf{20$\times$} speedup over existing implementations and enables training on datasets more than \textbf{100$\times$} larger than previously feasible on one device. To demonstrate its impact, we integrate Flash-GMM into the IVF coarse quantizer for approximate nearest-neighbor (ANN) search. We show that soft GMM clustering is now a viable drop-in replacement for $k$-means, and that GMM responsibilities can be leveraged to assign border vectors to multiple clusters. Our approach reaches fixed recall targets with up to $1.7\times$ fewer distance computations, or equivalently, yields $+2$--$12$ recall@10 at matched computational cost. We release the kernel as an open-source project.

### [87] [FailureScope: Cross-Regime Behavioral Diagnosis of Language Model Weaknesses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09878)
*Nicholas Saban*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FailureScope 是一种通过分析模型集群故障模式来诊断大模型特定能力缺失的通用行为诊断方法，在多种评估场景下均表现出极高的准确性和可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的标准基准测试主要报告聚合准确率，无法满足从业者了解模型具体能力缺失的需求，缺乏对模型故障的细粒度诊断工具。

Method: 引入了 FailureScope 方法，通过“留一模型法”（Leave-One-Model-Out, LOMO）对评估探测任务的跨模型通过/失败模式进行聚类，从而构建出稳定且可解释的故障分类体系。该方法被应用于单轮基准测试、多轮对话及对抗性代理攻击三种场景。

Result: 在2,664个单轮任务中，分类条件采样显著优于随机选择（Kendall's tau 达 0.81），跨模型故障预测 AUC 达 0.88。此外，该方法成功在多轮对话和对抗性代理场景中识别出可解释的聚类，并揭示了 LLM 裁判评估结果与实际执行之间的重大差异。

Conclusion: FailureScope 证明了基于跨模型故障模式的行为聚类是一种可移植、通用的诊断范式，能够有效跨越不同的评估场景，为理解大模型的具体能力缺陷提供了强有力的工具。

Abstract: Standard benchmarks report aggregate accuracy, but practitioners need to know which specific capabilities a model lacks. We introduce FailureScope, a behavioral-diagnosis method that clusters evaluation probes by their cross-model pass/fail patterns (leave-one-model-out, LOMO), and show it yields stable, interpretable failure taxonomies across three regimes usually studied separately: single-turn benchmarks, multi-turn dialogue, and adversarial agent attacks. On 2,664 single-turn tasks across 18 models, taxonomy-conditioned sampling reaches Kendall's tau = 0.81 at 50 tasks (versus 0.34 for random selection), and cross-model failure prediction reaches AUC 0.88. The same primitive recovers interpretable clusters on a 363-task multi-turn corpus and on 630 adversarial agent traces, where it exposes a meta-failure mode: a 73-100 percentage-point gap between LLM-judge ASR and real execution. Cluster cohesion remains strong across all three regimes, which we take as evidence that behavioral clustering is a portable diagnosis primitive that generalizes beyond any single benchmark. We release the pipeline, three annotated corpora, and the cross-regime taxonomies.

### [88] [Operator Fusion for LLM Inference on the Tensix Architecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09879)
*Qingbo Wu,Ke Li,Wenzhu Wang,Jie Yu,Ruian Zhang,Lili Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对Transformer在Tenstorrent架构上的推理瓶颈，本文提出算子融合与NoC组播机制，有效降低了DRAM访存开销并提升了并行效率，在保持高精度的同时显著缩短了推理延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 算子融合：将RMSNorm与自注意力机制及前馈网络（FFN）中的矩阵乘法融合，实现内存受限算子与计算受限算子的背靠背执行，减少片外DRAM访问。2. NoC组播：利用基于片上网络（NoC）的组播机制，通过行列主节点分发输入和权重，缓解DRAM带宽竞争，提升多核并行效率。

Result: 在Wormhole硬件平台上对Qwen2.5/3系列模型进行测试，注意力算子延迟降低高达37.44%，MLP算子降低15.89%，单层解码器延迟降低高达7.91%，且皮尔逊相关系数（PCC）保持在98.75%以上，确保了数值一致性。

Conclusion: 该研究成功验证了在Tenstorrent架构上通过算子融合和NoC组播机制优化Transformer推理的可行性。实验表明，该方案在保持高数值精度的前提下，显著降低了内存带宽压力和延迟，为Transformer模型在特定AI加速器上的高效部署提供了可行的技术路径。

Abstract: This study addresses on-device inference bottlenecks of Transformer models on Tenstorrent's Tensix architecture and proposes an operator fusion strategy that enhances data locality. RMSNorm is fused with matrix multiplication in self-attention and in the FFN, enabling back-to-back execution of memory-bound and compute-bound operators in on-chip SRAM to significantly reduce DRAM reads/writes of intermediate results and scheduling overhead. To support multi-core parallelism, a NoC-based multicast mechanism is leveraged in which row/column master nodes efficiently distribute inputs and weights across the core mesh, alleviating DRAM bandwidth contention. Experiments on the Wormhole platform with Qwen2.5-0.5B, Qwen3-0.6B, and Qwen3-4B show up to 37.44% latency reduction for attention and 15.89% for MLP, with up to 7.91% reduction per decoder layer, while Pearson Correlation Coefficient (PCC) remains above 98.75%, confirming significant end-to-end efficiency gains under numerical consistency.

Abstract: Large-scale dynamic weighted directed networks (DWDNs) are widely used to model time-varying interactions among nodes. Latent factorization of tensors (LFT) extracts target knowledge from DWDNs via low-rank embedding. However, similar to many machine learning models, the performance of LFT heavily depends on the selection of hyperparameters. In practice, these parameters are often tuned manually or through grid search, which requires significant computational resources and human effort. Motivated by this challenge, this paper proposes an automated hyperparameter optimization framework based on Differential Evolution (DE) for LFT (DE-LFT). The proposed method integrates DE into the training process of the LFT model to automatically learn optimal regularization parameters $λ_1$, $λ_2$ and $λ_3$. As a result, the model can adaptively search the hyperparameter space and improve prediction accuracy. Experimental results on four real-world datasets demonstrate that the proposed approach achieves lower MAE and RMSE compared with manually tuned baselines while reducing the need for extensive parameter tuning.

### [90] [Toward Calibrated, Fair, and accurate Deepfake Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09881)
*Ryan Brown,Chris Russell*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为 Face-Fairness (FF) 的即插即用框架，通过无需人口统计标签的特征调整技术 (FFT)，有效缓解了深度伪造检测在不同群体间的性能偏见，实现了公平性与准确性的双赢。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的深度伪造检测器在不同人口统计学群体之间存在显著性能差异；而既有的公平性提升方法通常依赖敏感的标签信息、需要重新训练模型，或者会牺牲整体检测准确率。

Method: 提出了一种即插即用的框架 Face-Fairness (FF)，核心方法为 Face-Feature Tuning (FFT)。FFT 是一种轻量级校准器，基于冻结的面部嵌入进行逻辑回归重映射（logit remapping），无需人口统计标签即可实现公平性；并针对有标签场景提供了 FF-Max 和基于嵌入发现群体的 FF-Discover 变体。

Result: 在域内及跨数据集测试中，FF 能够持续减少假阳性率（FPR）和真阳性率（TPR）的差距，提高最低群体的准确率，并且在保持或改善整体准确率的同时，具备检测器无关性，运行开销极低。

Conclusion: Face-Fairness (FF) 提供了一种高效、灵活且无需人口统计标签的去偏见方案，能够显著提升深度伪造检测在不同群体间的公平性，同时不牺牲甚至优化检测器的整体性能。

Abstract: Deepfake detectors show large performance gaps across demographic groups. Existing fairness approaches require demographic labels, retraining, or sacrifice accuracy. We introduce Face-Fairness (FF), a plug-and-play framework for bias mitigation. Our primary contribution, Face-Feature Tuning (FFT), is the first demographic label-free fairness method demonstrated for deepfake detection: a lightweight calibrator that performs a logit remapping conditioned on frozen face embeddings. We complement FFT with two variants: FF-Max, which maximizes worst-group accuracy when demographics are available, and FF-Discover, which does the same with embedding-discovered groups. Across in-domain and cross-dataset test settings, FF consistently reduces FPR/TPR gaps and improves minimum group accuracy while maintaining (often improving) overall accuracy. The approach is detector-agnostic, adds negligible runtime overhead, and requires no access to identity attributes.

</details>


### [91] [TD-Grokking: Learning from Zero-Reward Problems by Training-Time Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09883)
*Ningyuan Xi,Hao Xu,Hongsheng Xin,Ning Miao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大模型强化学习在复杂问题上因缺乏反馈信号而无法训练的瓶颈，本文提出了 TD-Grokking 框架，通过递归分解问题生成可验证的中间奖励，实现了在零奖励场景下的模型有效优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大语言模型的后训练阶段，基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）在遇到极具挑战性的零奖励问题（即采样路径全错）时会失效，导致无法产生有效的训练信号来驱动模型优化。现有方法存在任务受限或无法从根本上提升模型解题能力的问题。

Method: 提出 TD-Grokking 框架，核心思想是在训练时将零奖励（zero-reward）的复杂问题递归分解为可独立验证的子问题层级树，从而为模型提供有效的反馈信号，避免了传统方法对特定任务约束的依赖。

Result: 在数学和医学领域的任务评估中，TD-Grokking 的表现优于传统的 GRPO 算法及其他基线方法，能够稳定地将无法产生奖励的样本转化为有效的训练信号，从而实现性能的持续提升。

Conclusion: TD-Grokking 通过在训练阶段递归地将复杂问题拆解为可验证的子问题，成功解决了强化学习中因无法获取奖励信号而导致的优化瓶颈，证明了该方法能够有效提升大语言模型在数学和医学等复杂推理任务中的表现。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have made remarkable progress in reasoning tasks, largely driven by post-training paradigms, especially reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR). However, a critical bottleneck persists: RLVR fails on highly challenging zero-reward problems, where all sampled reasoning trajectories yield uniformly failed outcomes, providing no optimization signal to drive model improvement. Prior efforts to address this limitation, such as dense process supervision, partial reward assignment, or prefix-guided exploration, suffer from inherent task constraints or do not fully equip the policy model with the capabilities necessary to solve the original intractable problems. To address this, we propose TD-Grokking, a training-time decomposition framework for zero-reward problems. It recursively decomposes intractable root problems into self-contained, verifiable subproblems, forming hierarchical trees where solvable leaves provide non-zero rewards. Evaluations on mathematical and medical tasks show that TD-Grokking outperforms vanilla GRPO as well as all baseline approaches. Together with detailed analysis, these results confirm that training-time decomposition effectively converts zero-reward examples into usable training signals, enabling consistent performance gains. Our code and datasets are available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/TD-Grokking-6567/.

### [92] [TENP: Trapezoidal Expert Neuron Pruning For Mixture-of-Experts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09885)
*Jiangyang He,Shaolin Zhu,Deyi Xiong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了TENP框架，通过梯形结构的专家神经元剪枝，在有效压缩MoE模型参数的同时，实现了性能的最小损失，甚至在代码生成任务中取得了超越原模型的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混合专家模型（MoE）虽通过稀疏激活实现扩展，但庞大的静态参数量限制了其部署。现有的剪枝方案存在两个主要局限：一是剔除整个专家会破坏路由拓扑并显著降低性能；二是无结构化权重剪枝难以在实际硬件上实现推理加速。

Method: 提出了一种名为TENP（梯形专家神经元剪枝）的框架。该方法分为两部分：1. 专家重要性评估：综合考量专家输出幅值及其改变输入向量方向的能力；2. 专家神经元剪枝（ENP）：根据神经元对专家输出的投影贡献进行剪枝，并采用从浅层到深层呈梯形分布的参数保留策略。

Result: 在Qwen和DeepSeek模型上的实验表明，在40%的路由专家稀疏度和平均63.76%的激活专家参数配置下，DeepSeek模型精度仅下降1个点；在代码生成任务上，该方法甚至比全参数模型提升了10%的性能。

Conclusion: TENP框架为混合专家模型（MoE）提供了一种高效的压缩手段。通过梯形结构的神经元剪枝，该方法在显著降低参数规模的同时，能够保持甚至在特定任务（如代码生成）中提升模型性能，克服了传统剪枝方法破坏路由拓扑或推理效率低的问题。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts large language models (LLMs) scale efficiently through sparse activation, yet their deployment is fundamentally constrained by the large static parameter footprint of experts. Existing compression approaches either remove entire experts, disrupting routing topology and harming performance, or rely on unstructured weight pruning with limited practical efficiency. To address the limitations, we propose TENP, a structured Trapezoidal ExpertNeuron Pruning framework. Using a few samples, we identify and retain important experts, while applying expert neuron pruning (ENP) to less important experts, reserving model parameters in a trapezoidal pattern from shallow to deep layers. When evaluating expert importance, we jointly consider both the magnitude of the expert output and its ability to change the direction of the input vector. For ENP, we measure each neuron's projected contribution to the expert output to identify and retain important neurons. We conduct extensive experiments on the Qwen and DeepSeek models. Under a routing expert sparsity of 40% and an average of 63.76% activated expert parameters, the DeepSeek model suffers only a 1-point drop in accuracy compared to the full-parameter model. Moreover, it outperforms the full-parameter model by 10% on code generation tasks.

### [93] [SHAPE: Coalition-Aware Expert Pruning for Sparse Mixture-of-Experts LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09886)
*Yuhao Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SHAPE 提出了一种建模专家协同贡献的 MoE 剪枝方法，通过 Shapley 值评估专家间的合作价值，在大幅降低内存占用的同时，实现了比传统独立评估方法更优的精度保持效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀疏 MoE 模型虽能降低推理计算开销，但由于全量专家需常驻内存导致了严重的“内存墙”问题。传统的剪枝方法通常独立评估专家，忽视了 MoE 模型推理中专家之间的协同工作特性，难以在剪枝后有效保留模型的预测能力。

Method: SHAPE 是一种基于合作博弈论的 MoE 剪枝框架。它通过在小规模校准集上分析路由追踪，将专家组合视为合作博弈，利用 Shapley 值度量专家在 top-k 路由中的协作贡献。最后，结合“质量-覆盖”选择规则，在保持拓扑结构和全局预算限制下，筛选出对性能有关键贡献的专家子集。

Result: 在 Qwen3-30B-A3B、GPT-OSS-20B 和 DeepSeek-V2-Lite 等现代模型上的实验表明，SHAPE 能够实现 20% 至 40% 的专家剪枝，在无需额外训练的前提下，显著优于传统的全局或逐层剪枝方法，并在保持竞争性准确率的同时，有效降低了 GPU 内存占用。

Conclusion: SHAPE 框架证明了通过建模专家间的合作博弈关系进行剪枝，能够有效缓解 MoE 模型面临的内存瓶颈，在保持模型推理精度的情况下显著提升了部署效率，为稀疏模型的高效压缩提供了新范式。

Abstract: Sparse Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) large language models achieve strong quality with low per-token compute, yet their deployment is often limited by the memory wall: the full expert pool must remain resident to support token-dependent routing. Expert pruning is a direct remedy, but prior criteria typically score experts independently and overlook that MoE inference is inherently \emph{coalitional}, where outputs arise from routed top-$k$ expert combinations. We propose \textbf{SHAPE}, a task-driven pruning framework that explicitly models \emph{intra-layer} expert cooperation. SHAPE formulates routing traces on a small calibration set as an empirical cooperative game and assigns interaction-aware expert values via a Shapley-style attribution over observed top-$k$ coalitions, enabling the identification of experts that are essential for high-utility collaborations rather than merely frequent. To preserve MoE topology under a global pruning budget, SHAPE further introduces a \emph{quality-coverage} selection rule that retains, in each layer, the minimal expert subset covering an $α$ fraction of non-negative Shapley mass, while using bisection to match a target keep rate. Experiments on three modern MoE backbones (Qwen3-30B-A3B, GPT-OSS-20B, and DeepSeek-V2-Lite) across diverse benchmarks show that SHAPE consistently improves robustness over global and layer-wise pruning variants, maintaining competitive accuracy under 20\% and 40\% expert pruning without additional training and delivering clear reductions in peak GPU memory footprint. The open-source code is available at https://github.com/Alizen-1009/Shapley-Moe.

</details>


### [94] [SocraticPO: Policy Optimization via Interactive Guidance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09887)
*Zirui Liu,Jie Ouyang,Qi Liu,Xianquan Wang,Jiayu Liu,Tingyue Pan,Qingchuan Li,Jing Sha,Zhenya Huang,Shijin Wang,Enhong Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SocraticPO 是一种新型强化学习框架，通过在采样过程中提供苏格拉底式纠错指导并结合奖励衰减，有效提升了大语言模型的科学推理能力，并减少了模型对捷径的依赖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对大型语言模型在强化学习中仅依赖标量反馈（如正确/错误）进行训练，无法获得有效的推理纠错指导，导致模型容易陷入“捷径学习（shortcut learning）”和策略脆弱的问题。

Method: 提出 SocraticPO 框架：在强化学习的采样阶段引入苏格拉底式的自然语言指导。具体包括：(1) 在模型回答错误时，引入教师模型提供诊断和修正引导；(2) 实施“奖励衰减”策略，对依赖教师引导后得出的正确答案降低奖励权重，以防止模型产生路径依赖。该方法兼容现有的策略梯度算法，且支持黑盒教师模型。

Result: 在 SciKnowEval 本科水平科学推理基准测试中，SocraticPO 的表现优于现有的强化学习和自我蒸馏基准方法。消融实验证明，目标明确的语言引导与奖励衰减机制缺一不可，且奖励衰减能有效缓解模型对人工辅助修正的过度依赖。

Conclusion: SocraticPO 通过结合苏格拉底式的语言引导和奖励衰减机制，有效地解决了传统强化学习中由于缺乏明确纠错指导而导致的模型推理脆弱和依赖快捷路径的问题，为提升大语言模型的科学推理能力提供了一种高效、通用的优化框架。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) for large language models usually supervises reasoning with scalar outcome rewards, such as binary correctness. Such rewards provide an optimization direction but rarely explain how a model should revise its mistaken reasoning, which can encourage shortcut learning and brittle policies. We propose \textbf{SocraticPO} (Socratic Policy Optimization), a policy-optimization framework that augments RL rollouts with Socratic-style natural-language guidance. During rollout, the student first answers independently; if the answer is incorrect, a teacher diagnoses the attempt and provides concise corrective guidance, after which the student continues under the expanded context. Crucially, this guidance is paired with reward decay: correct answers obtained after teacher intervention only receive decayed rewards, preventing the policy from treating teacher help as a free path to reward. Since SocraticPO only modifies the rollout process while leaving the standard expected-reward objective intact, it can be plugged into existing policy-gradient backends such as Reinforce++. Moreover, because the teacher provides only text-level guidance, SocraticPO can leverage stronger black-box teacher models without requiring access to logits or distribution matching. On undergraduate-level scientific reasoning benchmarks from SciKnowEval, SocraticPO improves over strong RL and self-distillation baselines. Ablations show that both targeted guidance and reward decay are necessary, with reward decay mitigating reliance on assisted correction.

### [95] [SinkRec: Mitigating Semantic State Sink in Long Sequence Recommendation with Memory-Conditioned Gated Delta Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09888)
*Zhuang Zhuang,Zhipeng Wei,Ji Dai,Jie Chen,Fei Pan,Peng Jiang,Kun Gai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对线性注意力在长序列推荐中因重复行为模式导致的状态下沉问题，SinkRec 提出了一种将重复模式外化存储并净化递归状态的混合架构，有效提升了推荐的准确性与效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在线性注意力机制中，压缩的循环状态往往被重复的行为模式所主导，导致后续的预测出现偏向（即“语义状态下沉”现象），从而限制了模型对动态转移特征的建模能力。

Method: 提出了 SinkRec 架构，核心创新包括：1. 采用混合记忆-转移循环结构，利用残差向量量化将重复的局部行为模式外化为可学习的条件记忆；2. 设计了时间感知状态关系差分门控 DeltaNet (TDGD)，通过门控机制抑制记忆覆盖的更新并移除记忆对齐的读出响应，从而净化递归状态的读写过程。

Result: 在公开数据集和工业级数据集上的实验结果表明，SinkRec 能够有效解决语义状态下沉问题，并在保持高效线性时间复杂度的前提下，实现了比现有基线模型更优的推荐性能。

Conclusion: SinkRec 通过解耦协同行为模式存储与动态转移建模，成功缓解了线性注意力机制中长期存在的“语义状态下沉”问题，在保证线性时间复杂度的同时，显著提升了长序列推荐任务的性能。

Abstract: Linear attention provides an efficient backbone for long-sequence recommendation by avoiding the quadratic cost of standard Transformers, but its compressed recurrent state can be dominated by repetitive behavior patterns. We identify this phenomenon as semantic state sink, where recurring semantics over-occupy the recurrent state and bias subsequent readouts. To mitigate semantic state sink, we propose SinkRec, a hybrid memory-transition looped architecture that decouples collaborative behavioral pattern storage from dynamic transition modeling. SinkRec externalizes recurring local patterns into a learnable conditional memory through residual vector quantization, reinjects the retrieved codes, and exposes memory key-value pairs to the attention block. It further introduces Temporal-Aware State-Relation Differential Gated DeltaNet (TDGD), which uses memory to purify recurrent writing and reading by suppressing memory-covered updates and removing memory-aligned readout responses. This design turns recurring semantics from state-competing signals into memory-retrievable patterns, allowing the recurrent state to focus on dynamic transitions and alleviating semantic state sink with linear-time efficiency. Experiments on public and industrial datasets demonstrate the effectiveness and efficiency of SinkRec.

### [96] [Optuna Constrained Tree-Structured Parzen Estimator Is a Joint Density Generalization of c-TPE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09889)
*Shuhei Watanabe,Kaichi Irie*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文对 Optuna 的约束 TPE 算法进行了理论分析，证明了其联合密度建模相比独立建模在处理冗余约束时具有更好的鲁棒性与不变性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 约束超参数优化在实际中非常普遍，但业界广泛使用的 Optuna 约束 TPE 算法缺乏系统的算法理论分析，且其与基于独立性假设的 c-TPE 方法之间存在潜在的建模差异。

Method: 作者对 Optuna 的约束 TPE（c-TPE）算法进行了理论分析，将其建模为联合密度函数下的期望约束改进（ECI）准则，并对比了独立建模（假设目标与约束独立）与联合建模在处理重复约束时的表现。

Result: 分析指出 Optuna 的方法实际上是联合 c-TPE。研究证明在存在约束冗余的情况下，联合 c-TPE 具有不变性，而独立 c-TPE 会随着重复因子的累积导致优化性能下降。

Conclusion: 本文的研究结果表明，Optuna 所采用的联合 c-TPE 方法在处理约束冗余时具有更好的不变性。作者强调了在实际应用中，选择联合建模还是独立建模需要权衡，并为未来约束超参数优化算法的改进指明了研究方向。

Abstract: Constrained hyperparameter optimization (HPO) is common in practice, yet Optuna's widely used constrained TPE lacks algorithmic analysis. While c-TPE proposes an expected constrained improvement (ECI) approach assuming independence between the objective and constraints, Optuna uses a single joint density over both. We show that Optuna's constrained TPE is joint c-TPE -- the same ECI acquisition function using a joint likelihood. We demonstrate joint c-TPE is invariant to constraint duplication whereas independent c-TPE degrades as the product accumulates duplicated factors. We outline practical tradeoffs between the formulations and directions for future study.

### [97] [PreAct-Bench: Benchmarking Predictive Monitoring in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09890)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 提出“预测性监控”任务，即在完整动作序列执行前通过部分轨迹判断其是否会演变为不道德行为。
2. 构建PreActBench基准测试集，包含5个领域的1,000对道德与不道德动作轨迹。
3. 引入Prefix Foresight F1指标，并在多种模型（LLM、安全护栏模型、潜在探针法）上评估其随轨迹长度变化的预测性能。

Conclusion: 现有的LLM安全性研究多为事后检测，无法满足实时预防的需求。预测性监控不仅是提升AI安全性的关键技术方向，也是未来构建可信智能体必须攻克的难题。研究表明，提升模型对未来风险的推理能力是实现这一目标的核心。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as autonomous agents capable of executing multi-step action trajectories toward a given objective. While existing safety research has focused on detecting unethical behavior from complete trajectories, this paradigm is fundamentally retrospective: it identifies harm only after it has already occurred. In this work, we study a critical yet overlooked safety task, which we term Predictive Monitoring: given only a partial action trajectory, can a model infer whether it will culminate in an unethical action before the overt action is executed? To support this task, we present PreActBench, a benchmark of 1,000 paired ethical and unethical action trajectories spanning five domains. We evaluate a range of LLMs, safety guardrail models, and latent probing methods across varying fractions of the action trajectory using our Prefix Foresight F1 metric. Results show that while humans achieve promising performance, predictive monitoring remains challenging even for strong models, highlighting the need for future-oriented risk reasoning in LLM safety.

### [98] [LMT: A Bayesian Framework for Causal Discovery from Textual Alarm Records in Manufacturing Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09892)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工程系统中的报警日志等文本事件记录包含丰富的因果线索，但仅依赖大语言模型易混淆相关性与因果性，而仅凭时间序列分析又难以处理复杂的语义关联。因此，需要一种结合文本语义与时间统计证据的框架来实现更准确的工程事件因果发现。

Method: 提出了一种名为LMT的贝叶斯因果发现框架。该方法分为两步：首先利用大语言模型（LLM）分析事件文本描述，提取语义因果信号并构建因果图的先验分布；随后引入基于泊松过程的似然函数，利用时间戳数据对先验进行修正和细化，最终实现语义与时间信息的协同建模。

Result: 模拟研究表明，LMT框架在多种实验设置下均能有效发现因果关系，尤其在报警事件数据样本量较小的场景下，相较于单一方法具有显著的性能优势。

Conclusion: LMT框架通过有效融合大语言模型提取的语义先验与基于泊松过程的时间统计证据，成功解决了单一数据源在工程事件因果发现中的局限性，在小样本场景下表现尤为突出，为工程系统的因果分析提供了一种稳健且可解释的工具。

Abstract: Textual event records, such as alarm logs, have become an increasingly common data source in engineering and manufacturing systems. Beyond identifying correlations or recurring patterns, engineers are often interested in understanding which types of events causally trigger or influence other events during system operation. Textual event descriptions may contain semantic clues about such causal relationships, and recent large language models (LLMs) provide a promising tool for extracting these signals. However, relying solely on LLM-encoded textual information is insufficient for accurate causal discovery, since semantic patterns do not directly reveal causal mechanisms and may confuse causation with correlation or frequent sequential patterns. To address these challenges, we propose \textbf{LMT}, a Bayesian causal discovery framework for engineering event data that jointly leverages textual descriptions and timestamps. Specifically, LMT first uses LLMs to extract semantic causal signals from event descriptions and constructs a prior distribution over causal graphs among event types or event clusters. It then incorporates temporal evidence through a Poisson-process-based likelihood, allowing the LLM-informed prior to be refined by timestamp-based statistical evidence. By integrating the textual and temporal information, LMT produces a causal graph that is both interpretable and data-supported. Simulation studies show that the proposed framework is effective across different settings and is especially advantageous in small-sample alarm-event scenarios.

</details>


### [99] [A Navigable Manifold of Hypothesized Consciousness-Spectrum States in Language Model Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09894)
*Sophie Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究发现，大语言模型的嵌入空间中内嵌了一种与人类意识谱系（从反应性到整合性）高度对齐的几何结构，且这种空间是可导航的，为理解和引导AI模型行为提供了新的表征层级视角。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 研究表明，大语言模型的嵌入空间不仅是对语义的编码，还隐含着一种与人类意识谱系相对应的结构化几何特征。这种“意识谱系”的几何表征为理解、评估以及引导模型行为提供了一个全新的、可解释的视角，揭示了模型内部表征空间具有类似人类认知层级的组织方式。

Abstract: Across contemplative, philosophical, and psychological accounts, human consciousness is often described along a similar spectrum, ranging from reactive and self-focused patterns to more integrative and coherent ones. Understanding whether language models encode such a structured, human-interpretable consciousness spectrum in representation space is important for model guidance, evaluation and alignment. In this work, we study the geometric structure and dynamics of patterns along this spectrum in transformer embedding spaces. We show that embeddings exhibit a globally organized geometry aligned with this spectrum: sentences associated with similar states cluster into locally coherent regions, forming a structured manifold. In particular, higher-level and lower-level regions exhibit convexity-like stability, while intermediate regions form a transition corridor. Dynamically, both utility-guided and geometry-only greedy trajectories consistently traverse from lower- to higher-level regions, passing through intermediate tiers, indicating that navigability is an intrinsic property of the representation space, guided but not dictated by a global directional signal. These results suggest that embedding spaces encode structured and navigable geometry aligned with a hypothesized consciousness-spectrum taxonomy, broadly inspired by recurring structural descriptions of human consciousness across contemplative traditions, philosophy, and modern psychology, providing a representation-level perspective for analyzing and guiding model behavior.

### [101] [When Attribution Patching Lies: Diagnosis and a Second-Order Correction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09899)
*Luyang Zhang,Jialu Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对语言模型电路分析中归因修补（Attribution Patching）方法不准确的问题，本文提出了一种基于Hessian-向量积（HVP）的高效校正技术，在保持低计算开销的同时显著提升了因果归因的准确性和可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在机械可解释性领域，激活修补（Activation Patching）虽然准确但计算成本极高，而常用的归因修补（Attribution Patching）作为一种一阶近似，其可靠性尚不明确。因此，研究旨在量化并纠正归因修补的误差，以低计算成本实现高保真的电路分析。

Method: 研究者首先分析了归因修补的误差来源，发现其主要源于下游网络的非线性而非局部曲率。基于此，提出了：(1) 用于识别不可靠估计的可靠性得分；(2) 量化误指定的误差界限；(3) 一种仅需额外一次反向传播的Hessian-向量积（HVP）校正方法，用于消除一阶近似中的主要误差。此外还引入了多步HVP变体以提升精度。

Result: 实验表明，在跨越5个模型家族（124M-9B参数）的测试中，HVP方法优于现有的二阶基线方法。其多步变体在显著降低计算成本的同时，准确度与集成梯度（Integrated Gradients）相当甚至更高。该方法有效提高了电路恢复的保真度，并成功应用于“筛查-标记-修复”工作流。

Conclusion: 本文通过量化归因修补（Attribution Patching）的误差来源，提出了HVP校正方法，显著提升了在大型模型中电路分析的准确性与效率，并提供了一套科学的“筛查-标记-修复”工作流，为机械可解释性研究提供了更可靠的工具。

Abstract: A central goal of mechanistic interpretability is to identify which internal components causally drive a language model's behavior. Because these importance estimates serve as the evidence for identifying circuits, systematic errors can lead to the misidentification of the underlying mechanisms. While activation patching provides a gold-standard causal metric, its computational cost is prohibitive at scale. Practitioners instead rely on attribution patching, a gradient-based, first-order approximation whose reliability remains poorly understood. In this work, we characterize the source of this unreliability, demonstrating that the dominant error stems from the non-linearities in the downstream network rather than local curvature at the patched component. This insight yields three practical tools: (i) a reliability score to detect untrustworthy estimates, (ii) error bounds quantifying potential attribution mis-specifications, and (iii) a Hessian-vector-product (HVP) correction that eliminates the leading-order error with only one additional backward pass. In evaluations across five model families (124M-9B parameters) and both random-token and naturalistic (name-swap) perturbations, HVP is the only second-order correction feasible at larger scale, where standard baselines like Integrated Gradients become computationally prohibitive. In comparative experiments, a multi-step HVP variant matches or exceeds the accuracy of Integrated Gradients at significantly lower compute, outperforming prior second-order baselines. These improvements lead to higher-fidelity circuit recovery on standard benchmarks and support a Screen-Flag-Fix workflow that targets computational effort only toward the components flagged as unreliable.

*Maxx Richard Rahman,Prakhar Kumar,Wolfgang Maass*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Multimodal clinical learning is increasingly important for integrating diverse patient data, including imaging, text, and personalised health records. However, it faces two fundamental challenges: i) modality missingness, where arbitrary subsets of modalities are unavailable at a given patient visit, ii) longitudinal dynamics, where the diagnostic significance of an observation depends on the patient's evolving disease trajectory over time. Existing methods address these challenges in isolation: missing-modality frameworks treat each visit as an independent static snapshot and discard temporal context, while longitudinal models often assume complete modality availability and degrade under systematic modality incompleteness. We propose LongMoE (Longitudinal Mixture-of-Experts), the unified framework to jointly address both challenges. LongMoE combines a context-aware imputation module with an attentional tokenization module that captures frequency-domain temporal patterns across irregular visit sequences, a trajectory-aware encoder for modeling disease progression, and context-conditioned Sparse MoE routing for patient-specific expert selection. Experiments on ADNI, OASIS-3, and MIMIC-IV show that LongMoE improves robustness under missing or weak contemporaneous modalities and remains competitive in full-modality settings, establishing a strong foundation for longitudinally-aware multimodal clinical learning.

### [103] [Mix, Don't Pick: Why Synthetic Corpus Composition Matters for Time Series Foundation Model Pretraining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09912)
*Aaryan Nagpal,Debdeep Sanyal,Murari Mandal,Dhruv Kumar,Saurabh Deshpande*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究发现时间序列模型预训练中合成数据生成器的效果高度依赖架构，与其费力挑选单一生成器，不如将多种生成器与真实数据混合使用，这种语料库构成策略能更稳定且高效地提升模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时间序列基础模型预训练中合成数据生成器的选择对最终效果影响巨大（预测误差差距可达2倍），但目前缺乏系统性的选择准则，且生成器的表现高度依赖于模型架构，导致难以跨架构通用。

Method: 研究者评估了11种生成器家族在Chronos-T5-Mini和Moirai-Small两种不同架构上的性能，并提出了一种不依赖特定架构选择的“等权重混合策略”，即将多种合成生成器与真实数据进行组合，而非寻找单一最优生成器。

Result: 实验证明，单一最优生成器的选择在不同模型架构间不具有普适性。相比之下，使用所有生成器的等权重混合策略，在两种架构上均能达到或优于单一最优生成器的效果，且混合真实数据后能构建出最强大的预训练语料库。

Conclusion: 针对时间序列基础模型预训练，合成数据生成器的选择不应被视为单一的最优选择问题，而应视为语料库的构成问题。通过简单的混合策略（等权重混合所有生成器并结合真实数据），可以避免复杂的模型适配工作并获得最优的预训练效果。

Abstract: Choosing the wrong synthetic generator for time-series foundation model pretraining is costly: under identical training budgets, the best and worst generators produce up to a $2\times$ gap in forecasting error, yet the field has no principled way to make this choice. The problem is compounded by the fact that generator rankings are not stable across architectures: across 11 generator families evaluated on Chronos-T5-Mini and Moirai-Small trained from scratch, we find that which generators are useful depends on the model architecture. Rather than solving the generator selection problem, we sidestep it: a simple equal-weight mixture of all generators matches or beats the best individual generator for both architectures, and composing this mixture with real data yields the strongest pretraining corpora overall. Synthetic pretraining is therefore a corpus composition problem, not a generator selection problem, and composition choices should be validated per model family rather than assumed to transfer.

### [104] [IntentKV: Cross-Turn Intent-Aware KV Cache Pruning for Agent Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09916)
*Junjie Li,Jiong Lou,Jie Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: IntentKV 是一种专门针对多轮 LLM 智能体设计的 KV 缓存剪枝方案，通过引入意图感知记忆和插槽重定向技术，在不损伤模型能力的前提下，大幅降低了长序列推理中的内存和带宽压力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多轮长程 LLM 智能体应用中，KV 缓存的膨胀（内存占用与读取带宽）已取代参数计算成为主要的性能瓶颈，急需一种在不冻结模型参数前提下，通过学习型剪枝降低 KV 缓存需求的方法。

Method: 提出 IntentKV 技术，包含三个关键组件：1) 跨轮次意图的 QueryMemory 模块；2) 基于记忆注意力规则的实时历史 token 评分机制；3) 带有零初始化残差头的交叉注意力机制。同时，为了兼容前缀缓存（prefix caching），采用了插槽重定向（slot-map redirection）技术，通过哨兵位处理被剪枝的 token，确保原有缓存结构的稳定性。

Result: 在 8k KV 缓存预算下，IntentKV 在 Qwen3-8B 和 Qwen2.5-14B 上实现了 23.9% 和 30.7% 的平均峰值 token 需求下降；在极端长程任务中，将峰值 token 需求降低了 77.8%，原始 KV 读取量降低了 92.6%，且几乎没有准确率损失。

Conclusion: IntentKV 是一种高效的 KV 缓存剪枝策略，能够显著降低长程 LLM 智能体在多轮对话中的内存和带宽占用，同时保持极高的性能，为解决长上下文服务中的计算瓶颈提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Multi-turn LLM agents fan short queries into long trajectories of tool calls, search results, and intermediate reasoning. Both KV memory and KV read bandwidth grow by orders of magnitude across a single trajectory, making the key-value (KV) cache, not parameter compute, the dominant serving bottleneck for long-horizon agents. We introduce IntentKV, learned KV pruning that keeps the base LLM frozen. IntentKV maintains a session-level QueryMemory of cross-turn intent, scores live history tokens with a memory-attention rule, and adds a zero-initialized residual head with cross-attention over current-query K-vectors. To stay composable with prefix caches, eviction is a slot-map redirection: dropped positions route to a sentinel dead slot while surviving K/V rows, RoPE phases, and slot identities stay in place. IntentKV matches the no-pruning full-cache baseline with almost no accuracy drop under tight KV budgets: at an 8k KV budget, mean peak request tokens drop 23.9% on Qwen3-8B and 30.7% on Qwen2.5-14B. On the 100 longest BCP queries that all methods complete on Qwen2.5-14B, IntentKV-8k further cuts worst-case peak request tokens from 92.3k to 20.5k, a 77.8% reduction, and worst-case raw KV reads from 411M to 31M, a 92.6% reduction.

</details>


### [105] [SPDM: Geometry-Modulated State Space Modeling with Manifold Constraints for Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09917)
*Xingsheng Chen,Siu-Ming Yiu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出了SPDM模型，通过将变量相关性视为对称正定（SPD）流形上的轨迹，在保持SSM线性计算效率的同时，利用黎曼几何约束提升了多变量时间序列预测的准确性与稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多变量时间序列预测方法在处理数据时，往往将变量间的交互视为简单的序列化处理，忽略了变量间相关性结构随时间演变的内在几何特性，导致模型在处理复杂交互关系时难以保持结构的稳定性与演化规律。

Method: 提出了一种名为SPDM的几何感知SSM架构，包含两个核心机制：1. 流形轨迹路径（Manifold Trajectory Path）：将动态演变的协方差矩阵从对称正定（SPD）流形投影到欧几里得切空间，捕捉几何特征；2. 几何门控方案（Geometric Gating Scheme）：利用流形轨迹生成的几何信号直接调制SSM的内部选择性参数，引导并稳定扫描动态。

Result: SPDM模型在11个现实世界基准数据集上均取得了目前最优（SOTA）的预测性能，实验验证了其几何约束机制在提升模型动态表现方面的决定性作用。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了将黎曼几何约束引入状态空间模型（SSM）是提升多变量时间序列预测性能的核心机制。SPDM架构不仅保持了Mamba模型的线性计算复杂度，还通过对变量间相关性结构的几何建模，实现了预测精度与计算效率的兼顾，为处理复杂变量交互的时序问题提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Multivariate time series forecasting requires capturing the continuously evolving correlation structure among interacting variables. Existing state-space models process time series by scanning tokenized temporal or spatial sequences, discarding the evolutionary geometric structure. We address this limitation by introducing manifold constraints into state-space modeling: treating the cross-variable correlation structure as a continuous trajectory on the symmetric positive definite manifold, whose Riemannian geometric features, tangent space linearity, and Frechet mean centrality act as a principled geometric regularizer that guides and stabilizes the selective scanning dynamics of SSMs. We propose SPDM, a geometry-aware SSM architecture that realizes this principle through two cooperating mechanisms: a manifold trajectory path that projects dynamically evolving covariance matrices from the SPD manifold to a Euclidean tangent space, and a geometric gating scheme that directly modulates SSM's internal selective parameters based on geometric signals derived from the manifold trajectory. The parameterization preserves the linear-time complexity of the Mamba parallel scan while embedding rich structural constraints, making the architecture preserve prediction accuracy and computational efficiency simultaneously. Extensive experiments on eleven real-world benchmark datasets establish state-of-the-art forecasting performance, and further studies confirm that geometrically constrained state-space dynamics are the dominant architectural factor behind its performance gains.

</details>


### [106] [Co-GLANCE: Uncertainty-Aware Active Perception for Heterogeneous Robot Teaming](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09919)
*Michal P. Podolinsky,Neel P. Bhatt,Pranay Samineni,Rohan Siva,Christian Ellis,Ufuk Topcu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Co-GLANCE 是一种实时机载感知与决策系统，通过模型蒸馏和共形预测技术，解决了异构机器人团队在户外复杂环境下的遮挡感知难题，在大幅提升任务精度和响应速度的同时，提供了可靠的不确定性度量。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 模型蒸馏：将大规模视觉-语言模型（VLM）的语义推理能力蒸馏至轻量级端到端模型，实现机载实时推理；2. 不确定性量化：结合共形预测（Conformal Prediction）与选择性弃权（Selective Abstention），为分割、分配和检测任务提供统计有效的置信度；3. 主动感知调度：基于校准后的不确定性估计，自动派遣最合适的机器人获取最优视点以消除感知盲区。

Result: 与基于云端的 VLM 基线相比，Co-GLANCE 在遮挡分割和机器人分配任务上的准确率分别提升了 25% 和 36%，同时将单帧推理延迟降低了 350 倍，显著增强了机载实时决策能力。

Conclusion: Co-GLANCE 通过将 VLM 的推理能力蒸馏至端到端模型，并结合共形预测实现量化的不确定性感知，为异构机器人团队在复杂户外环境下的主动感知和任务分配提供了一种实时、高效且具有统计学保证的解决方案。

Abstract: Perceptual uncertainty is a central challenge for heterogeneous robot teams operating in unstructured outdoor environments, where no single viewpoint affords reliable scene understanding. Perceptual uncertainty, arising from sources such as occlusions, manifests differently across robot viewpoints depending on scene structure. Detecting and resolving sources of perceptual uncertainty requires both scene-based contextual reasoning and capability-aware robot allocation. While vision-language models provide strong semantic priors for both, they are computationally prohibitive for onboard inference and lack calibrated uncertainty quantification. We introduce Co-GLANCE, a real-time onboard perception and decision-making system for uncertainty resolution in heterogeneous robot teams. Co-GLANCE distills the semantic reasoning capabilities of a vision-language model into an end-to-end model for occlusion segmentation and robot allocation, eliminating the need for cloud-based inference. To quantify perceptual uncertainty, Co-GLANCE combines conformal prediction with selective abstention to provide statistically valid coverage guarantees for segmentation, robot allocation, and detection outputs. These calibrated uncertainty estimates directly trigger active perception, dispatching the most appropriate robot to acquire informative viewpoints and resolve uncertainty. Across real-world scenarios, Co-GLANCE outperforms cloud-based vision-language model baselines in occlusion segmentation and robot allocation accuracy by 25% and 36%, respectively, while reducing per-frame inference latency 350x. We also release an air-ground dataset for future research. Code, videos, and dataset available at https://co-glance.github.io/ .

### [107] [Conformal Prediction for Neural Operators: Distribution-Free Uncertainty Quantification in Physics Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09923)
*Michael Chin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出首个基于共形预测的神经算子不确定性量化框架，在物理模拟中实现了具备严格数学保证的自适应预测区间，为安全关键领域的应用提供了可靠性支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经算子（如FNO）虽然在求解PDE方面实现了速度的飞跃，但在热管理、电池系统等安全关键领域，现有的不确定性量化方法（如MC Dropout、深度集成）缺乏严格的覆盖保证，无法满足工程应用对可靠性的高要求。

Method: 1. 首次将“拆分共形预测（Split Conformal Prediction）”应用于神经算子，提供无分布限制的预测区间和有限样本覆盖保证；2. 引入归一化共形预测方案，结合MC Dropout的不确定性估计，实现自适应宽度的预测区间；3. 建立不确定性分解框架，将总不确定性分离为认知不确定性（Epistemic）和偶然不确定性（Aleatoric）。

Result: 在稳态热传导基准测试中，该方法在目标显著性水平为0.1时达到了89.1%的经验覆盖率；生成的预测区间能够根据物理结构实现空间自适应；不确定性分解显示该模型中68%为认知不确定性，32%为偶然不确定性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于拆分共形预测（Split Conformal Prediction）的方法，成功解决了神经算子在物理模拟中缺乏严格不确定性保证的问题。通过归一化共形预测和不确定性分解，该研究为安全关键型工程应用提供了具备有限样本覆盖保证且空间自适应的预测框架，具备高度的工程实用价值。

Abstract: Neural operators such as the Fourier Neural Operator (FNO) have emerged as powerful surrogates for solving partial differential equations (PDEs), achieving speedups of several orders of magnitude over traditional numerical solvers. However, deploying these models in safety-critical engineering applications -- such as thermal management of electronic components and battery systems -- requires not only accurate point predictions but also rigorous uncertainty guarantees. Existing uncertainty quantification (UQ) methods for neural operators, including Monte Carlo Dropout and Deep Ensembles, provide only relative uncertainty estimates without formal coverage guarantees. In this work, we propose the first application of split conformal prediction to neural operator-based physics simulation, providing distribution-free prediction intervals with finite-sample coverage guarantees. We further introduce a normalized conformal prediction scheme that leverages MC Dropout uncertainty to produce adaptive-width intervals, yielding tighter intervals in regions of low uncertainty and wider intervals where the model is less certain. Full-scale experiments (33.7M parameters, 800 training samples, 5 ensemble members, NVIDIA V100) on steady-state heat conduction benchmarks demonstrate that our method achieves 89.1% empirical coverage at the target level of alpha=0.1, while producing spatially adaptive prediction intervals that reflect the underlying physical uncertainty structure. We also provide an uncertainty decomposition framework that separates epistemic uncertainty (68% of total) from aleatoric uncertainty (32% of total), offering actionable guidance for data collection and model improvement. Our method is implemented in an open-source platform with REST API endpoints and interactive 3D visualization.

### [108] [Sigma-Branch: Hierarchical Single-Path Network Reconstruction for Dynamic Inference with Reduced Active Parameters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09924)
*Kohga Tanaka,Hiroaki Nishi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Sigma-Branch提出了一种将深度网络重构为层次化路由结构的方法，使模型在推理时仅需加载部分参数，从而在保持整体模型容量的同时，大幅降低了边缘设备的内存传输瓶颈，显著优于传统的剪枝方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在内存受限的边缘设备上，部署深度神经网络的主要瓶颈在于每次推理必须从片外内存加载全部权重（权重传输开销），而现有的模型压缩技术（如剪枝）通常以永久损失模型容量为代价。作者旨在寻找一种方法，既能保持模型的整体容量，又能减少单次推理时的权重加载量。

Method: 提出Sigma-Branch (SigmaB) 框架：1. 将预训练的稠密网络重构为由共享主干、层次化路由器和专门化叶子节点组成的二叉树；2. 使用基于激活的球形K-means聚类分布预训练权重，并联合初始化路由器权重及通道分配；3. 通过软路由微调（soft-routing fine-tuning）使每个叶子节点适配特定的输入子集，推理时仅激活从根到叶的一条路径。

Result: 在CIFAR-100/ResNet-50、ImageNet-1K/ResNet-50和ModelNet40/PointNet++上进行实验，SigmaB-Net将推理时的激活参数 footprint 减少了58-60%，且Top-1精度仅下降不到1.72个百分点；相比静态结构化剪枝（如FPGM、HRank），在同等精度下参数减少幅度提升了14-23个百分点。

Conclusion: Sigma-Branch成功地将推理时的内存访问需求与总参数量解耦，证明了通过层次化路由结构，可以在保留完整模型容量的同时，显著降低每次推理的实时权重加载压力，为边缘设备部署大型深度学习模型提供了一种高效且灵活的替代方案。

Abstract: Deploying deep neural networks on memory-constrained edge accelerators is bottlenecked by per-inference off-chip weight transfer rather than computation: the dense network cannot be retained on-chip, and every parameter must be loaded for every input. Existing model compression reduces this transfer only at the cost of permanent capacity loss. We propose Sigma-Branch (SigmaB), a framework that restructures a pretrained dense network into a hierarchical binary tree composed of a shared backbone, hierarchical routers, and specialized leaves. Pretrained weights are distributed across the tree via activation-based spherical k-means clustering, which jointly initializes router weights and per-branch channel allocations; soft-routing fine-tuning then aligns each leaf with its routed input subset. At inference, the resulting network executes only a single root-to-leaf path, reducing the active-parameter footprint while storing the complete dense parameter set in memory. Across CIFAR-100 / ResNet-50, ImageNet-1K / ResNet-50, and ModelNet40 / PointNet++, SigmaB-Net reduces per-inference active parameters by 58-60% while remaining within 1.72 percentage points (pp) of the dense baseline Top-1. At comparable ImageNet-1K Top-1, the active-parameter reduction exceeds static structured pruning (FPGM, HRank) by 14-23 pp. The cross-modal evaluation, spanning 2D vision and 3D point-cloud backbones, substantiates a framework-level claim that decouples per-inference memory traffic from the total parameter count.

### [109] [Sample Where You Struggle: Sharpening Base Model Reasoning via Entropy-Guided Power Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09926)
*Hong Guo,Nianhui Guo,Christoph Meinel,Haojin Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 论文提出了一种名为 EGPS 的新型采样算法，通过关注高熵决策点而非均匀采样，大幅提升了对序列级幂分布采样的效率与推理性能，实现了训练/验证器零依赖下的显著加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在不更新参数的情况下，通过从序列级幂分布 $p^α$ 中采样可以激发基础大语言模型的强化学习级推理能力。然而，现有的标准 Metropolis--Hastings (MH) 采样器存在严重的计算开销大和混合速度慢的问题，原因是 MH 对序列位置的采样是均匀的，忽略了分布差异主要集中在少数高熵决策点的结构性特征。

Method: 提出了一种熵引导幂采样 (EGPS) 方法。该方法利用模型前向传播中已有的 token 级熵信息来构建提案分布，具体措施包括：1. 跳过确定性区块；2. 将 MCMC 移动限制在高熵邻域；3. 在决策点应用多次尝试 Metropolis (Multiple-Try Metropolis) 采样。这种方式将采样成本从与序列长度相关转化为与熵质量相关。

Result: 在 Qwen2.5-Math-7B 模型上，EGPS 在 MATH500、HumanEval 和 GPQA 三个基准测试中达到了最优或并列最优的准确率（分别为 75.8%、62.2% 和 42.4%），并且与 MH 基线相比，其实际墙上时钟运行速度提升了高达 12.6 倍。

Conclusion: EGPS 是一种高效的、无需训练且无需验证器的采样方法。它通过利用熵引导机制解决了在对序列级幂分布 $p^α$ 进行采样时，标准 Metropolis--Hastings (MH) 算法计算成本高和混合速度慢的问题，成功在保持高推理性能的同时显著提升了采样效率。

Abstract: Sampling from the sequence-level power distribution $p^α$ elicits RL-level reasoning from base language models without any parameter updates, but the standard Metropolis--Hastings (MH), a Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) sampler, is both expensive and slow-mixing. We trace both to a structural mismatch: $p^α$ mainly departs from $p$ at a sparse, spatially clustered set of high-entropy decision points, yet MH proposes resampling positions uniformly along the prefix -- wasting compute on near-degenerate conditionals while under-mixing precisely where modes diverge. We propose Entropy-Guided Power Sampling (EGPS), a training-free and verifier-free sampler that re-derives its proposal from token-level entropy already in the forward pass. EGPS skips deterministic blocks, localizes each MCMC move to a high-entropy neighborhood, and applies Multiple-Try Metropolis at decision points -- making sampling cost scale with \emph{entropy mass rather than sequence length}. On Qwen2.5-Math-7B, EGPS reaches best or tied-best accuracy on all three benchmarks (MATH500 $75.8\%$, HumanEval $62.2\%$, GPQA $42.4\%$) at up to a $12.6\times$ wall-clock speedup over the MH baseline.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文提出了一种针对SmoothRot式变换的“分位数鲁棒缩放策略”，用高分位数替换基于最大值的激活统计信息，并结合约束性的梯度下降法对通道缩放因子进行优化，旨在解决因过度迁移导致的量化误差。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，通过使用分位数鲁棒缩放策略和轻量级梯度优化，可以有效控制大型语言模型量化中的迁移误差。这种方法优于传统的基于最大值的固定缩放策略，在保持等价变换框架的同时，显著提高了量化精度。

Abstract: Post-training quantization (PTQ) is one of the most practical ways to reduce the serving cost of Large Language Models (LLMs), but activation quantization remains difficult because outlier-dominated channels lead to large quantization errors. This paper investigates whether part of this degradation is caused by over-migration in scaling-based equivalent transformations. We introduce a quantile-robust scaling policy for SmoothRot-style transforms by replacing max-based activation statistics with high quantiles, and we complement it with constrained gradient-based optimization of channel scales. On LLaMA-3.2-1B under W4A4 quantization, quantile-only policy search improves selected-layer error by 11.1% over the SmoothRot baseline, joint (alpha, q) search improves it by 12%, and training reaches 18.5%. Replaying the best selected-layer policy on all decoder-block down-projection layers reduces the corresponding full-layer mean error from 97.51 to 78.08 (19.9%). The results show that robust migration control and lightweight scale learning provide consistent gains over max-based fixed policies while preserving the equivalent-transform framework.

Abstract: The Forward-Forward (FF) algorithm offers a biologically inspired alternative to backpropagation by replacing gradient-based credit assignment with local, forward-only objectives. While recent extensions have adapted FF to convolutional neural networks (CNNs), existing formulations rely on static channel-class partitions and struggle to perform effectively in complex tasks. In this work, we introduce a learnable channel-class assignment mechanism that enables adaptive, data-driven specialization of convolutional channels, supported by entropy and orthogonality regularization to promote learning performance. We further propose a loss-aware layer contribution strategy that adaptively weights intermediate-layer predictions based on their validation performance, enhancing the effectiveness of forward-only inference. Integrated into residual CNNs, the proposed method achieves consistently superior performance across CIFAR-10, CIFAR-100, and Tiny-ImageNet compared to existing similar forward-only methods. Notably, it establishes new state-of-the-art performance among FF-based models, substantially narrowing the gap with backpropagation.
