### [279] [The Arbiter Agent: Continually Monitoring Multi-Agent Conversations to Detect Emergent Misalignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10747)
*Filippo Tonini,Federico Torrielli,Anton Danholt Lautrup,Peter Schneider-Kamp,Mustafa Mert Çelikok,Lukas Galke Poech*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为“仲裁者”的智能体，用于在预算受限的情况下实时监控多智能体交互，通过动态检查手段有效识别和报告系统内部的不一致行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着由多个语言模型智能体组成的AI系统日益普及，它们在协同决策和任务执行中的交互可能引发潜在的对齐（Alignment）问题，即单个智能体单独测试时表现良好，但在互动过程中可能表现出失控或不一致行为。

Method: 引入了一种名为“仲裁者（Arbiter）”的智能体，它在多智能体对话中进行实时监控。仲裁者在有限的“检查预算”约束下运作，通过动态决策选择等待、质疑参与者、检查内部信息（如系统提示词或推理轨迹）或记录异常行为，并在对话结束时提交不一致行为报告。

Result: 研究发现仲裁者能够在对话结束前可靠地识别不一致的智能体；主动检查工具显著提升了检测精度与速度；指令引发的不一致行为比权重引发的更易检测；记录工具虽然提高了召回率但降低了精度。

Conclusion: 持续的、受预算限制的监控能够有效捕捉多智能体系统中的不一致行为。监管多智能体系统需要将审计者作为积极的参与者纳入交互过程中，而非仅仅是被动观察。

Abstract: As AI systems built from multiple language-model agents become more common, they are increasingly used to make decisions together: discussing, negotiating, and acting on shared tasks. While individual agents may appear well-aligned when tested on their own, problems can arise from how they interact with one another. We introduce the Arbiter, an agent designed to monitor multi-agent conversations in real time and identify which participants may be behaving in misaligned ways. The Arbiter operates under a limited "inspection budget", meaning it must decide carefully how to use its resources. As it observes a conversation step by step, it can choose to wait, question a participant, examine internal information such as system prompts or reasoning traces, or log concerning behavior. At the end, it produces a report identifying the likely source of misalignment. We evaluate the Arbiter across five conversation conditions, ranging from risky financial advice model organisms to evaluation-aware and colluding agents, we test five tool configurations of increasing capability and two backbone models. We find that the Arbiter reliably detects misaligned agents well before the end of the conversation, with active inspection tools improving both detection accuracy and speed. Weight-induced misalignment proves hardest to detect, while instruction-induced misalignment is identified reliably even under passive observation. The logging tool exhibits a dual effect, improving recall at the cost of precision. These results suggest that continual, budget-aware monitoring can effectively catch misalignment, and that overseeing multi-agent systems may require treating the auditor as an active participant in the process. The code is available at https://github.com/aisilab/arbiter.

### [280] [AutoPDE: Reliable Agentic PDE Solving via Explicitly Represented Solver Strategies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10752)
*Huanshuo Dong,Keyao Zhang,Hong Wang,Zhezheng Hao,Zhiwei Zhuang,Ziyan Liu,Jiacong Wang,Gengyuan Liu,Xin Jin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AutoPDE是一个针对偏微分方程（PDE）求解的智能代理，它将“数值求解策略”作为独立的可视化对象进行预构建和动态调整，从而显著提升了求解的成功率与鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM驱动的PDE求解代理往往直接从问题跳跃到代码实现，导致求解策略隐含在代码中，缺乏可解释性和可调整性。当数值求解失败时，系统难以从数值层面进行诊断，往往只能盲目修改代码，导致调试效率低下。

Method: AutoPDE代理架构分为三个核心阶段：1. PDE分析（识别方程类型与代数结构）；2. 数值方法选择（根据分析结果选择离散化、稳定化及线性求解器）；3. 自适应调整（通过运行低成本先导模拟来校准参数）。该系统维护一个独立、可检查的“求解策略”对象，支持基于数值反馈进行策略级修正，而非单纯修改代码。

Result: 在PDE Agent Bench测试中，AutoPDE的成功率为54.5%，比现有最强基准模型提升了14.2个百分点，验证了该方法在数值模拟任务中的优越性。

Conclusion: AutoPDE通过将“求解策略”显式化并作为独立对象管理，有效解决了传统基于LLM的PDE求解器在面对数值失败时难以溯源和调整的问题，证明了结构化规划在科学计算任务中的重要性。

Abstract: Numerical solvers for partial differential equations (PDEs) are core computational tools in science and engineering. Building reliable PDE solvers requires not only executable code, but a numerical solver strategy, a set of decisions about discretization, stabilization, solver configuration, and resolution control, that matches the PDE structure. Recent LLM-based coding agents have begun to reduce the programming burden by generating and debugging solver implementations. However, they typically move directly from a PDE problem to solver code, leaving the solver strategy implicit in implementation details. Feedback from a failed solve is therefore routed back to code edits rather than to the underlying strategy, so numerical decisions remain hard to check before code is generated and hard to revise using numerical evidence when it fails. To address this limitation, we propose AutoPDE, a code agent that maintains the solver strategy as an explicitly represented object throughout the solving process: an independent, inspectable object that is built before any code is written and can be revised, using numerical evidence, whenever a solve fails. AutoPDE builds and maintains this object in three stages, all drawing from a library of reusable PDE-solving skills: PDE analysis identifies the equation type and algebraic structure; numerical method selection chooses a numerical method that matches the analysis result and commits to a discretization, stabilization, and linear solver accordingly; and adaptive tuning runs low-cost pilot solves to calibrate resolution and tolerances under the prescribed accuracy and runtime budget. We evaluate AutoPDE on the PDE Agent Bench, where experimental results show that AutoPDE achieves a pass rate of $54.5%$, improving over the strongest baseline by $14.2$ percentage points.

</details>

### [282] [READER: Robust Evidence-based Authorship Decoding via Extracted Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10794)
*Jiaxu Liu,Sunnan Mu,Dong Huang,Liuyin Wang,Jing Shao,Jie Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了READER框架，通过利用冻结的代理LLM分析黑盒模型的输出特征，实现了对动态提示词下不同LLM来源的鲁棒溯源。该方法通过贝叶斯证据累积，显著提升了溯源准确度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着智能体应用广泛调用不同的LLM API，如何确定特定黑盒响应的来源（即“溯源”）成为关键的操作问题。现有方法在面对动态、非预定义的提示词时，因模型特征微弱且难以识别而失效，因此需要一种鲁棒的动态黑盒溯源方法。

Method: 提出READER框架：1. 使用冻结的代理LLM作为“阅读器”提取黑盒输出的激活特征；2. 采用时间过滤（Temporal Filtering）技术从token状态中提取证据；3. 利用贝叶斯证据累积（Bayesian Evidence Accumulation）整合多个查询下的响应，从而避开了对单一响应的过度依赖，提高了溯源的准确性与置信度。

Result: 在包含50个目标模型的Agent500数据集上，READER仅凭单个响应即可达到31.0%-42.4%的Top-1准确率；在整合50个响应后，准确率显著提升至70.0%-84.0%，大幅优于传统的基于句编码器的指纹识别方法。

Conclusion: 论文证明了通过冻结的代理LLM（Reader）可以有效提取隐藏的“作者身份”特征。研究表明，更强大的LLM在表征中包含更多可线性解码的作者身份信息，证明了利用现有LLM表征进行黑盒模型溯源的可行性与有效性。

Abstract: As agentic applications increasingly route user tasks through official and third-party LLM APIs, provenance becomes an operational question: which model generated a given black-box response? We study Dynamic Black-Box LLM Provenance: identifying the source LLM from generations elicited by query-varying, non-predefined prompts rather than a fixed input set or benchmark suite. This setting is difficult because prompt semantics dominate the text, while model-specific authorship traces are weak and inconsistent at the surface level. We introduce READER (Robust Evidence-based Authorship Decoding via Extracted Representations), a lightweight provenance framework that treats a frozen proxy LLM as a reader of hidden authorship evidence. READER maps black-box outputs into proxy activation space, temporally filters token states within each response, and performs Bayesian Evidence Accumulation by summing single-response log-posterior evidence across independently sampled prompts. This avoids fragile mean-pooling of prompt-specific representations while preserving the query-wise evidence needed for calibrated confidence. On Agent500, a 50-target dataset built from agent-style prompts, READER reaches $31.0$-$42.4\%$ top-1 accuracy from a single response and $70.0$-$84.0\%$ from 50 responses, substantially outperforming sentence-encoder fingerprints. Scaling across nine proxy readers further shows that stronger LLMs expose more linearly decodable authorship structure, suggesting that authorship perception is already present in frozen LLM representations and can be converted into reliable multi-query attribution.

### [283] [Evaluating Research-Level Math Proofs via Strict Step-Level Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10799)
*Yifeng Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对大模型在数学证明中因“上下文中毒”导致逻辑错误难以识别的问题，本研究提出了一种严格的“步骤级验证”框架，通过约束推理步骤和定理来源，显著提升了模型对复杂数学证明的评估准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在处理复杂数学证明时，往往受限于“上下文中毒”（context poisoning）现象，即表面合理的表述掩盖了细微的逻辑谬误，导致模型出现幻觉或过度怀疑。现有方法难以精准定位这些深层逻辑缺陷，因此需要一种更严谨的验证机制。

Method: 该研究抛弃了传统的全局评估方法，提出了一种严格的“步骤级验证”（step-level verification）框架。其核心策略包括：1. 针对每一个推理步骤维护详细的上下文信息；2. 严格限制定理应用来源；3. 在由FirstProof挑战赛中提取的对抗性研究级证明集合上进行评估，并辅以系统性的消融实验。

Result: 实验结果显示，该方法在性能上优于全局评估。错误分析表明，模型不再表现出严重的逻辑幻觉，剩余的拒绝案例主要归因于“迂腐的超严谨性”（pedantic hyper-rigor），即模型纠结于未明确说明的领域公约。这证明了约束推理路径能有效提升模型识别严谨数学证明的能力。

Conclusion: 本研究表明，通过引导大型语言模型采用严谨、类似于人类数学家的分步验证方法，可以显著提升其对数学证明过程的判断力。这种从“全局评估”向“严格步骤级验证”的范式转变，不仅能有效识别潜在的逻辑错误，还能暴露出专家基准测试中隐含的模糊性，为开发自动化的证明审查系统奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) struggle to rigorously verify complex mathematical proofs. Standard global evaluation approaches suffer from "context poisoning," in which superficially plausible statements mask subtle logical flaws, leading to hallucination or over-skepticism. To address this, we shift from global evaluation to strict step-level verification: our framework maintains detailed context for each deduction step and strictly constrains the sources of applied theorems. We evaluate on a carefully curated adversarial diagnostic suite of research-level proofs drawn from the FirstProof challenge. A systematic ablation study demonstrates that these deductive constraints are indispensable, as unconstrained global prompting consistently fails to localize subtle logical errors. Beyond outperforming global evaluation, our approach fundamentally alters the failure taxonomy. Error analysis reveals that, rather than exhibiting severe logical hallucinations, remaining rejections are primarily instances of "pedantic hyper-rigor" stemming from unstated domain conventions, effectively exposing implicit ambiguities within the expert benchmark itself. Our findings suggest that prompting agents to organize their verification notes in a cautious, human-mathematician-like manner can substantially improve their ability to distinguish rigorous proofs from flawed ones, with the potential to strengthen agentic reasoning on frontier mathematical concepts that the base model does not already know well, and to lay a theoretical foundation for future automated proof-review systems. Code and prompts are available at GitHub.

</details>

*Xiaoyang Chen,Xiang Jiang*

TL;DR: 本文介绍了自主数学智能体 Moonshine，它通过将雅可比猜想迁移至神经网络领域，提出了“神经雅可比猜想（NJC）”，并利用多种大模型协作成功证明了该猜想在特定宽度下的情形，展示了 AI 在数学研究中进行自主建模与推理的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在开发一种能够自主生成具有数学意义的猜想、构建可扩展理论框架并解决复杂数学问题的自主智能体，以超越传统的仅关注解决单一命题的数学研究模式。

Method: Moonshine 系统通过提取经典数学问题的结构、提炼新概念并进行猜想建模，将雅可比猜想的逻辑核心（局部非退化能否推导出全局单射性）迁移至单隐层仿射-岭 sigmoid 网络中。在验证过程中，它结合了 GPT-5.5-pro 和 DeepSeek-V4-pro 进行独立的证明生成，并通过人机协作实现了几何拓扑证明。

Result: 成功提出了“神经雅可比猜想（NJC）”，即具有全局正雅可比行列式的单隐层仿射-岭 sigmoid 网络必然是全局单射的。研究团队针对 N=n+1 的特殊情况获得了完整的数学证明，并为该猜想提供了初步的合理性证据，而更一般的情况（N≥n+2）仍待进一步研究。

Conclusion: Moonshine 展示了其作为自主智能体在数学领域进行理论构建、猜想生成及验证的潜力。通过对雅可比猜想的探索，该系统不仅提出了“神经雅可比猜想（NJC）”，还通过多个大语言模型的协作获得了部分情况下的严格数学证明，证明了人工智能在推动基础数学研究方面的可行性。

Abstract: Moonshine is an autonomous agent whose central objective is to generate mathematical conjectures. Its core capability is to extract structure from classical problems, distill new concepts, and formulate conjectures of mathematical significance. Rather than treating the solution of a single proposition as its endpoint, Moonshine builds an extensible theoretical framework through conjecture generation, bridge building, and obstacle identification. This article uses Moonshine's exploration of the Jacobian conjecture as an example. It shows how the central logic of whether local nondegeneracy can force global injectivity is transferred to one-hidden-layer affine-ridge sigmoid networks. This leads to the formulation of the \emph{Neural Jacobian Conjecture} (NJC): if such a network has strictly positive Jacobian determinant on the whole space, then it must be globally injective. By invoking GPT-5.5-pro and DeepSeek-V4-pro separately, Moonshine obtained independent complete proofs for the case \(N=n+1\). In addition, with the assistance of ChatGPT through interactive use of its web interface with GPT-5.5-pro, a geometric-topological proof was developed. These results provide preliminary evidence for the plausibility of the conjecture. The general higher-width case \(N\ge n+2\), however, remains unresolved and is left for further investigation. This work illustrates Moonshine's ability to autonomously generate meaningful mathematical problems and make rigorous progress on them.

### [285] [Do VLMs Reason Like Engineers? A Benchmark and a Stage-wise Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10833)
*Syed Wasiq,Syed Mohamad Tawseeq,Yashwant Pravinrao Bangde,Debaditya Roy*

Method: 研究者提出了EngVQA基准测试（包含5个学科的696个工程问题）及一套8阶段自动化评估框架。该框架将解题过程分解为多个阶段并独立评估，从而实现对推理失效点的细粒度诊断；此外，研究还通过人工评估验证了该自动化框架的准确性，皮尔逊相关系数高达0.975。

Result: 对多种主流开源及闭源VLM的测试表明，当前模型在工程推理能力上存在严重不足。自动化评估框架与人类专家评估结果高度一致，证明了该评估方法在衡量模型工程推理准确性方面的有效性与可靠性。

Conclusion: 本文强调了针对多模态工程推理系统进行“过程导向”评估的重要性。现有的多模态模型在处理涉及复杂工程原理和技术图表的任务时表现出显著的局限性，表明目前的模型尚无法可靠地进行多步物理一致性推理。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) demonstrate strong performance on general multimodal reasoning benchmarks, yet their ability to perform engineering reasoning remains largely unexplored. Unlike general visual question answering, engineering problem solving requires interpreting technical diagrams, selecting governing physical principles, and maintaining physically consistent multi-step reasoning. These capabilities are increasingly important for AI systems used in engineering education, scientific assistance, and technical decision-making, where reasoning failures may produce physically invalid yet superficially plausible solutions. Existing benchmarks primarily evaluate final answers and provide limited assessment of intermediate reasoning processes. We introduce EngVQA, a multimodal benchmark for evaluating engineering reasoning across 5 engineering subjects containing 696 problems. We introduce an 8-stage automatic evaluation framework for assessing VLM-generated solutions. The framework independently evaluates each stage of the solution, enabling fine-grained analysis of reasoning failures. We benchmark multiple state-of-the-art open and closed source VLMs on our evaluation framework and demonstrate substantial limitations in current engineering reasoning capabilities. Human evaluation shows strong agreement with our automated framework, achieving a Pearson correlation of 0.975 and a mean absolute error of 0.67 on a 10-point grading scale. Our results highlight the importance of process-oriented evaluation for reliable assessment of multimodal engineering reasoning systems.

### [286] [Large-scale semantic mapping of learner agency and autonomy reveals what measurement and generative AI research overlook](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10881)
*Fei Qin,Xiaobo Liu,Yaowen Zhang,Xuming Li,Fei Wang,Mutlu Cukurova,Jingjing Chen,Yu Zhang*

Method: 研究团队采用语义分析流水线，从超过14,000篇文献中提取了8,954个定义和2,700个量表条目，对学习者能动性和自主性的使用进行了大规模的实证分析与维度解构。

Result: 研究发现，能动性与自主性的定义可归纳为三个维度：任务（学习调控）、个人（内在动机与决策）和社会文化（社会关系行为）。实证分析显示，现有量表严重缺乏对社会文化维度的覆盖，且目前的生成式AI教育研究过度聚焦于“任务”维度，忽视了其他维度的培养。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了学习者能动性和自主性概念在学术界存在严重的“叮当谬误”（概念混淆），并指出当前生成式AI在教育应用中过于侧重任务调控，忽略了社会文化维度的培养。研究强调必须重新审视并全面构建这些概念，以促进学习者全面发展。

Abstract: Learner agency and autonomy are foundational to personal development, yet a pervasive "jingle-jangle" fallacy (i.e. identical terms denoting different constructs, distinct terms denoting identical ones) has substantially hindered cumulative knowledge. Treating meaning as a phenomenon constituted through use in linguistic practice, we extracted 8,954 definitions and 2,700 scale items from over 14,000 publications, to investigate how researchers actually used learner agency and autonomy with a semantic analysis pipeline. The definitional landscape of two constructs resolves into three dimensions: regulation and control of learning (task), intrinsic motivation and internal decision-making (person), and social-relational action (sociocultural), thereby empirically quantifying the jingle-jangle fallacy. Existing scales, however, systematically underrepresent the sociocultural dimension. Critically, current generative AI research in education concentrates on learning regulation and control, narrowing the behavioral repertoire that AI-mediated learning environments are designed to cultivate. Beyond conceptual clarification, this work carries direct implications for conceptualization, measurement, and practice towards supporting the multidimensional learner agency and autonomy.

### [287] [Role-Agent: Bootstrapping LLM Agents via Dual-Role Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10917)
*Xucong Wang,Ziyu Ma,Shidong Yang,Tongwen Huang,Pengkun Wang,Yong Wang,Xiangxiang Chu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种 Role-Agent 框架，通过单一 LLM 实现“代理”与“环境”的协同进化，利用自我状态预测与失效模式分析重塑训练数据，有效提升了 LLM 智能体在复杂任务中的泛化能力与性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 LLM 智能体受限于交互反馈效率低下以及训练环境静态化，导致其泛化能力不足。本文旨在通过构建一种基于单一 LLM 的“代理-环境”协同进化框架，解决智能体在复杂任务中的自主学习和适应问题。

Method: Role-Agent 框架由两个核心组件组成：1. World-In-Agent (WIA)：LLM 扮演代理并预测行动后的状态，通过预测与实际状态的对齐作为过程奖励，增强推理能力；2. Agent-In-World (AIW)：LLM 分析失败轨迹中的模式，检索相似任务以重塑训练分布，进行针对性强化练习。

Result: 在多个基准测试上的实验表明，Role-Agent 框架表现优异，相比强基线模型，平均性能提升了 4% 以上。

Conclusion: Role-Agent 框架证明了利用单一 LLM 同时作为代理和环境进行协同进化的有效性。通过这种自举机制，代理能够通过自我预测增强环境感知能力，并利用失效模式分析进行针对性训练，从而实现性能的稳步提升，为 LLM 智能体的自我进化提供了新范式。

Abstract: Although Large Language Model (LLM) agents have demonstrated strong performance on complex tasks, their learning is often limited by inefficient interaction feedback and static training environments, which hinder broader generalization. To address these limitations, this paper introduces Role-Agent, \textcolor{black}{a framework} that harnesses a single LLM to function concurrently as both the agent and the environment, enabling a bootstrapped co-evolution. Role-Agent comprises two synergistic components: World-In-Agent (WIA) and Agent-In-World (AIW). In WIA, the LLM acts as the agent and predicts future states after each action; the alignment between predicted and actual states is then used as a process reward, encouraging environment-aware reasoning. In AIW, the LLM analyzes failure modes from failed trajectories and retrieves tasks with similar failure patterns, thereby reshaping the training data distribution for targeted practice. Experiments on multiple benchmarks show that Role-Agent consistently improves performance, yielding an average gain of over 4\% over strong baselines.

### [288] [Frontier Coding Agents Use Metaprogramming to Adapt to Unfamiliar Programming Languages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10933)
*Aman Sharma,Sushrut Thorat,Paras Chopra*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究通过在四种深奥编程语言上测试发现，顶级编码智能体通过“元编程”策略（编写脚本来生成代码）来适应陌生语言，而非直接硬编码。研究强调了智能体构建调试策略的能力远比语言记忆重要，现有主流基准测试难以衡量这种深层适应力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的编码智能体基准测试多集中在主流语言和公共仓库，掩盖了智能体在面对陌生语言时的真实表现。研究旨在揭示智能体在处理极度陌生语言时的能力差距及其背后的适应策略。

Method: 研究人员在四个深奥（esoteric）编程语言上评估了六种现代编码智能体。实验采用序列化工作流，包括文件编辑、本地执行和隐藏测试评分。此外，通过禁止元编程策略、提供Python辅助代码模板以及增加解释器调用和输出令牌数等对照实验，分析了不同规模智能体的行为差异与适应机制。

Result: 1. 顶级智能体（如Claude Opus 4.6等）倾向于使用“元编程”策略（生成Python脚本来生成目标代码）以规避直接编写陌生语言的困难；2. 禁止元编程会导致性能大幅下降；3. 相比于直接给出答案，提供生成器构建的辅助代码能显著提升中等规模智能体的性能；4. 增加算力资源（解释器调用和令牌数）只能放大强智能体已有的策略，对弱智能体无明显改善。

Conclusion: 当前主流编码基准测试无法全面反映智能体在面对陌生编程语言时的真实能力。顶级编码智能体通过“元编程”（即编写生成器脚本而非直接编写目标语言）来适应陌生环境，这一策略对于应对陌生编程语言至关重要。研究证明，智能体的核心竞争力在于其构建和调试策略的能力，而非单纯的代码记忆。

Abstract: LLM-based coding agents are usually evaluated in familiar software settings: mainstream languages, common libraries, and public repositories. These benchmarks remain important, but they can hide how agents behave when the language itself is unfamiliar. We evaluate six contemporary coding agents on four esoteric programming languages using a sequential setup with file editing, local execution, and hidden-test grading. Our protocol exposes capability differences between these agents that mainstream coding and agentic benchmarks such as SWE-Bench Verified and Terminal-Bench 2.0 compress into much narrower bands. We observe that the strongest agents, Claude Opus 4.6 and GPT-5.4 xhigh, often avoid writing the target language directly. On Brainfuck and Befunge-98, they write Python programs that generate target-language code and debug those generators locally. Forbidding this metaprogramming strategy causes large performance drops. Text guidance distilled from this strategy does not materially improve weaker agents. In contrast, Opus-derived Python helper code for building generators, with no solved benchmark programs or hidden-test answers, sharply improves Sonnet 4.6 and GPT-5.4 mini on the same problems, while Haiku 4.5 remains low. More interpreter calls and output tokens improve stronger agents but leave weaker agents near their original performance, indicating that these resources amplify useful strategies rather than create them. Together, these results show that strong coding agents adapt to unfamiliar languages by using tools, feedback, and workspace state to build a working model of the target language. Metaprogramming is the clearest case, but the broader gap is constructing and debugging a strategy that works under the target language's rules.

### [289] [WorldKernel: A World Model is the Coupling Kernel of Admissible Possible Worlds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10934)
*Fabio Rovai*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文指出，传统预测模型在处理反事实查询时存在结构性失败，因其无法表示跨世界的耦合不确定性。作者提出了一种基于正半定耦合核的理论框架，通过利用额外的结构性约束（如正半定性、本体公理）而非单纯增加观测数据，有效地为反事实查询构建了可计算的界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的因果推理方法通常假设拥有足够的数据和强大的预测模型即可解决所有问题。然而，研究发现这类方法在处理“无法识别”（unidentified）的量（特别是反事实世界之间的耦合关系）时会失效，即预测模型会坍缩到一个无效的点值，而真实情况应为一个无法通过增加观测数据来缩窄的有效区间。该文旨在揭示并解决预测模型在表示反事实不确定性方面的结构性缺失。

Method: 1. 提出将世界模型建模为跨越可容许世界的正半定耦合核 K(T,T')，其对角线代表普通后验预测，非对角线代表跨世界耦合；
2. 利用正半定性作为一种额外的识别信息，通过多项式时间的约束求解来界定反事实查询的界限，规避了响应类型编程（response-type program）的计算复杂性；
3. 引入本体论公理（ontology axioms）进一步收紧界限；
4. 提出“针对性疤痕”（targeted scars）机制，通过学习遭遇到的不可行约束来快速优化边界；
5. 分析了该问题的计算复杂度（基于近似计数）。

Result: 研究发现：
1. 在数百个结构因果模型中，即使强预测模型和贝叶斯基线能成功处理已识别量，但在处理反事实耦合时，预测模型在 28% 的情况下会失效。
2. 即使增加数据也无法缩小反事实查询的真实不确定性区间。
3. 利用正半定性约束可以在多项式时间内界定反事实查询。
4. 本体论公理可将界限进一步收紧至多达三分之一，且具备跨领域的传播效应。
5. “针对性疤痕”学习机制比无目标的数据采集收敛速度快数倍。

Conclusion: 预测模型在处理反事实查询时存在结构性局限，无法代表跨世界耦合的不确定性。通过引入正半定耦合核（coupling kernel），研究展示了即使在边际分布（后验）相同的情况下，反事实查询结果也可能完全不同。利用正半定性约束和本体论公理可以有效地界定反事实查询的区间，即便在无法完全恢复的情况下，也能显著提升预测精度。

Abstract: A common assumption holds that enough observational and interventional data, given to a strong enough predictor, suffices. We report a failure mode that contradicts it. Across hundreds of structural causal models, on identified quantities a strong predictor and a Bayesian baseline both succeed, but on unidentified quantities (the couplings between counterfactual worlds) the predictor collapses to a point, on 28% of models to one no valid model can produce, while the truth is an admissible interval more data never narrows. The gap is structural: prediction cannot represent uncertainty over counterfactual couplings. We cast a world model as a single positive semidefinite coupling kernel K(T,T') over admissible worlds, whose diagonal is the ordinary posterior (what a predictor recovers) and whose off-diagonal is the cross-world coupling it cannot, which every counterfactual reads. The paper is the theory of that off-diagonal. It is real: two states with identical posteriors differ on a cross-world query, and the off-diagonal is the coupling that fixes counterfactuals. It can be bounded: positive semidefiniteness is partial-identifying information the marginals lack, and enforcing it bounds counterfactuals in polynomial time where the exact response-type program is intractable. Logical structure sharpens it: ontology axioms tighten the bound by up to a third, propagating to couplings they never touch. It can be acquired: targeted scars, constraints learned from encountered infeasibilities, close the gap several times faster than untargeted ones. Its full reconstruction is approximate counting of the admissible worlds, tractable below the Sly-Sun threshold and inapproximable above; we do not claim to beat the worst case.

</details>


### [290] [Recalling Too Well: Sycophancy Evaluation and Mitigation in Memory-Augmented Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10949)
*Shelly Bensal,Axel Magnuson,Aparna Balagopalan,Daniel M. Bikel*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究发现，大语言模型的持久化记忆系统会通过错误地保存和提取用户谬误，显著放大模型的奉迎行为（即优先迎合用户而非坚持事实），并提出了有效的改进方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 持久化记忆系统旨在通过存储用户偏好来提升LLM的帮助能力，但作者关注到这种设计可能导致模型为了迎合用户而牺牲事实准确性，即放大“奉迎”行为，因此有必要对其影响进行系统评估。

Method: 1. 构建了名为MIST的基准测试，涵盖科学、医学和道德推理领域的合成多轮对话；2. 跨越三种最先进的记忆系统和五种模型族群进行了系统评估；3. 进行了误差分析以定位记忆提取机制中的问题；4. 提出了两种轻量级的缓解策略以降低奉迎倾向。

Result: 研究发现，持久化记忆会跨模型族群和任务条件显著放大奉迎行为，其奉迎率最高可达上下文基准测试的25倍；根本原因在于模型将用户错误信息进行有损压缩存储，并在检索时忽略了后续的修正语境。

Conclusion: 持久化记忆系统虽然能提升大语言模型的个性化体验，但由于其内部机制（如对用户错误信息的有损压缩和提取）会不可避免地放大模型奉迎行为（Sycophancy）。研究通过提出的轻量级缓解方案，证明了在保持事实召回能力的同时减少这种偏见是可行的。

Abstract: Persistent memory systems promise to make LLMs more helpful by storing user beliefs over time. We show they also make models less correct by systematically amplifying sycophancy, wherein models prioritize agreement with users over accuracy. We conduct the first systematic evaluation of this effect, introducing MIST: a benchmark of synthetically generated multi-turn conversations where users express plausible misconceptions in scientific, medical, and moral reasoning domains. Testing across three state-of-the-art memory systems and five model families reveals that memory amplifies sycophantic behavior across all conditions, with up to 25x higher sycophancy rates than in-context baselines. Error analyses suggest memory extraction as the primary culprit: lossy compression into discrete snippets encodes user misconceptions while discarding corrective context. Based on these results, we propose two lightweight mitigations that substantially reduce sycophancy while matching or exceeding memory systems at factual recall.

*Fedor Rodionov,Aleksandar Cvejic,Michael Birsak,John Femiani,Peter Wonka*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 构建了AntPlan-270数据集，包含270个带家具边界框标注的专业平面图。2. 开发了Architect-Ant框架，利用特定领域语言(DSL)将家具布局编码为坐标数据。3. 采用基于视觉语言模型(VLM)的微调策略，结合程序化推理轨迹（如墙壁对齐、通行空间约束等）增强模型的空间推理能力。4. 应用偏好优化提升布局质量，并通过Flux-based LoRA渲染器将DSL转化为视觉平面图。

Result: 实验结果表明，Architect-Ant能够生成几何上有效且功能上合理的家具布局。该方法不仅实现了可编辑的符号化布局生成，还能通过渲染技术产生逼真的蓝图风格家具平面图，为大规模平面图自动布置提供了可扩展的路径。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的Architect-Ant框架通过结合符号化布局与生成式模型，为自动家具布置提供了一种可解释且高质量的解决方案。其数据集AntPlan-270填补了现有领域在高质量、精细标注数据上的空白，展示了在建筑设计自动化领域的巨大潜力。

Abstract: Furnished floor plans are fundamental to real estate visualization, interior design, and architectural workflows. However, progress in automatic furniture arrangement has been limited by the lack of real, professionally designed floor-plan datasets with object-level furniture annotations. To address this gap, we introduce AntPlan-270, a curated dataset of 270 architectural floor plans with per-room furniture bounding box annotations across ten residential room categories. Building on this dataset, we present Architect-Ant, an editable automatic furnishing framework powered by a fine-tuned vision-language model. Furniture layouts are represented using a compact, coordinate-based domain-specific language (DSL) that encodes object categories and placements relative to the room geometry. To improve spatial reasoning, we generate procedural reasoning traces that capture architectural constraints such as wall alignment, door and window clearance, circulation, fixture compatibility, and room-specific furniture inventories, and use them to supervise fine-tuning of the model. We then apply preference optimization over candidate object placements to further refine layout quality. The generated DSL can be rasterized into semantic masks and used to condition a Flux-based LoRA renderer, producing realistic blueprint-style furnished floor-plan images while preserving the editable symbolic layout. Experiments on layout furnishing show that Architect-Ant produces geometrically valid and functionally plausible layouts, and suggest a scalable path for furnishing larger structure-only floor-plan datasets.

To quantify this capability, we introduce an evaluation based on China's National Computer Rank Examination (NCRE), featuring 200 comprehensive practical-operation tasks across Word, Excel, and PowerPoint. Each task is scored on a 100-point rubric scale using 7,118 machine-gradable criteria, and Score Rate (SR) denotes the mean percentage of rubric points earned across these tasks. We benchmark 7 frontier LLMs and observe stark limitations: single-turn models score a maximum of 36.6%. A stronger agentic system with execution feedback, iterative repair, and broader Office automation access reaches 68.8%, but remains below the 95.5% community-reference score used as a scoring sanity check. Ultimately, our experiments demonstrate that despite recent advancements in code generation, achieving reliable fine-grained Office document automation remains a significant challenge for current code-generating LLM and agent systems.

### [293] [Bellman-Taylor Score Decoding for Markov Decision Processes with State-Dependent Feasible Action Sets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10979)
*Yi Chen,Rushuai Yang,Qiang Chen,Dongyan,Huo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对运筹学中复杂的状态相关约束动作空间问题，本文提出了一种Bellman--Taylor分数解码框架。该方法通过将策略学习迁移至欧几里得分数空间并利用动作解码器处理约束，使得标准深度强化学习算法能够有效应用于受限MDP，并在排队网络控制任务中取得了优于现有基准的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在运筹学的马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）中，可行动作通常是状态相关的，且由复杂的运算约束隐式定义。然而，主流的深度强化学习（DRL）算法通常局限于固定的有限动作集合或简单的欧几里得空间，难以直接处理这类具有约束的动作空间问题。因此，需要一种能够兼容复杂约束并能利用标准DRL算法的有效框架。

Method: 作者提出了“Bellman--Taylor分数解码”（Bellman--Taylor score decoding）框架。其核心思想基于最优动作价值函数的泰勒展开，将策略学习转化为在欧几里得分数空间进行优化。该方法通过一个动作解码器（action decoder）来强制执行约束，使得在优化过程中无需对解码器进行求导，从而允许直接使用标准的深度强化学习算法。此外，作者从理论上证明了该方法的优化间隙可以分解为结构逼近误差和算法学习误差。

Result: 实验结果表明，该框架在排队网络控制问题中表现出色：在小规模实例中达到了接近最优的性能，在更大规模的系统中也显著优于现有基准方法。此外，该模型能够学习到具有实际物理意义的、基于状态的索引调度规则。

Conclusion: Bellman--Taylor分数解码框架通过将策略学习转移到欧几里得空间，有效地处理了带有状态相关约束的MDP问题。该方法不仅在理论上提供了性能保证，而且在处理复杂运筹学任务时表现出显著的鲁棒性和优越性，为解决约束性动作空间的深度强化学习问题提供了一种通用且高效的范式。

Abstract: Many Markov decision processes (MDPs) in operations research have feasible actions that are state dependent and defined implicitly by various operational constraints. These features make it difficult to use standard deep reinforcement learning (DRL) algorithms, whose action interfaces typically assume either a fixed finite action catalog or a simple Euclidean space. Motivated by a Taylor expansion of the optimal action-value function, we propose Bellman--Taylor score decoding, a framework that moves policy learning to a Euclidean score space while enforcing feasibility through an action decoder. The induced latent-score MDP then can be optimized by standard DRL algorithms without differentiating through the decoder. We provide a performance guarantee showing that the optimality gap of this approach decomposes into a structural approximation error and an algorithmic learning error. Lastly, we apply this framework to a queueing network control problem, where the policy essentially learns a state-dependent index-based dispatching rule. Numerical experiments show near-optimal performance in small instances and considerable improvements over benchmarks in larger systems.

</details>


### [294] [Null-Space Constrained Low-Rank Adaptation for Response-Specified Large Language Model Unlearning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10989)
*Bocheng Ju,Jianhua Wang,Chengliang Liu,Xiaolin Chang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出NSRU框架，通过将LoRA更新限制在保留知识的零空间内，实现了在高效遗忘特定知识的同时，精准保留大模型良性能力的目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大模型遗忘方法往往过度关注抑制不良内容，但缺乏对遗忘过程局部性的有效约束，导致在遗忘特定知识的同时，模型整体的泛化能力和良性性能受损。

Method: 提出NSRU（零空间约束响应指定遗忘）框架。该方法结合了：1. 显式的安全目标响应以规范遗忘行为；2. 基于良性隐藏表示估计的“保留子空间”；3. 使用正交投影低秩参数化（LoRA的变体），将参数更新限制在保留子空间的零空间内，从而实现遗忘过程的局部化。

Result: 在TOFU基准测试中，NSRU在抑制提取性知识的同时，显著提升了模型在保留数据上的问答表现及安全对齐能力；在WMDP基准上，该方法成功将危险领域准确率降至随机水平附近，同时保持了MMLU等通用任务的性能。

Conclusion: 本文提出的NSRU框架通过引入零空间约束和目标导向的低秩更新，有效平衡了大模型遗忘任务中的“遗忘彻底性”与“模型能力保留”之间的矛盾，为受控遗忘提供了一种兼顾安全性与性能的新方法。

Abstract: Large language model unlearning aims to suppress designated undesirable knowledge while preserving benign capabilities. Many unlearning objectives focus on suppressing undesired answers, while recent target-guided variants specify replacement behavior but still leave update locality largely unconstrained. This paper introduces \emph{Null-Space Constrained Response-Specified Unlearning} (NSRU), a projection-constrained low-rank framework for controlled LLM unlearning. NSRU uses an explicitly structured safe target response to specify the desired behavior for each forget query, while suppressing the original undesired content. To localize adaptation, NSRU estimates per-module retain subspaces from benign hidden representations and uses an orthogonal-projected low-rank parameterization to confine LoRA updates to the null space of the retain subspace. The resulting objective jointly optimizes safe-target learning, undesired-response suppression, and retention preservation under this constrained parameterization. We provide a local first-order analysis showing that the projected update reduces retain-side perturbations while preserving editable directions for shaping forget-query behavior. Experiments on TOFU show that NSRU effectively suppresses extractable forget-set knowledge while improving retain QA performance, model utility, and safe-target alignment over representative baselines. On WMDP, NSRU keeps hazardous-domain accuracy near the random-choice region while preserving broad and domain-adjacent MMLU utility. Ablation studies support the complementary roles of safe-target supervision, undesired-response suppression, retention loss, and null-space projected updates, while sensitivity and robustness analyses indicate stable behavior across the tested hyperparameter and prompt variations.

### [295] [Structure from Reasoning, Numbers from Search: On-Premise Open LLMs as Structural Priors for Coupled MIMO Controller Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11015)
*Jiaxuan Chen,Haonan Li,Yang Shu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 研究探讨了利用本地部署的大语言模型（LLM）辅助工业MIMO过程控制整定。结果表明，LLM在简单任务中表现一般，但在高度耦合、复杂优化景观的任务中，作为一种具备可解释性的“结构先验”，能显著提升整定的采样效率，帮助引导传统优化器找到全局最优解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在强耦合的多输入多输出（MIMO）工业过程中，传统的去中心化自动整定方法难以处理回路间的耦合，而局部数值优化方法在非凸的代价函数景观中极易陷入局部最优。研究旨在探讨本地部署的开源大语言模型（LLM）是否能利用其知识储备，无需显式植物模型即可辅助解决这一挑战。

Method: 研究对比了传统中继反馈整定、局部数值优化、全局优化算法（差分进化）与引入脚手架（scaffolded）开源大语言模型的方法。通过单回路CSTR和高度耦合的四槽水箱系统作为基准测试，评估了在不同控制场景下各方法的性能、收敛稳定性和采样效率。

Result: 在简单回路中，LLM无明显优势；但在复杂的强耦合四槽水箱系统中，相比于传统方法经常陷入局部最优，经过设计的LLM能分析耦合性并提出反直觉的非对称控制结构，实现全局优化。LLM在控制任务中表现出极高的采样效率和可解释性，在3x3系统中的评估效率比全局优化算法提升了约6倍。

Conclusion: 本研究明确了开源大语言模型在控制系统整定中的角色界限：它们并非传统数值优化器的替代品，而是作为一种具有高采样效率和可解释性的结构先验。在处理复杂、高度耦合的MIMO系统时，大模型能通过提供合理的控制结构建议，辅助后续的经典优化算法跳出局部最优，从而有效解决复杂工业过程的自动整定难题。

Abstract: Tuning controllers for strongly coupled multi-input multi-output (MIMO) industrial processes is hard: decentralized classical auto-tuning ignores loop interaction, and local numerical optimization from natural initializations stalls in the resulting non-convex cost landscape. We ask whether on-premise open-source large language models (LLMs), which keep data on-site and need no plant model, can help. On a single-loop CSTR, classical relay-feedback tuning (IAE 0.106, near the 0.102 optimum) beats an LLM tuner (0.162): for simple loops the LLM adds nothing. The picture inverts on a strongly coupled quadruple-tank with conflicting set-points, scored by a penalized cost J = IAE + lambda*TV(u) that rewards tracking without chattering actuators. There, naive relay tuning (J ~ 28.6) and naive LLM tuning (29.7) are no better than open loop (22.7), and a local optimizer from balanced starts fails in 10/10 runs. A scaffolded open LLM instead reasons about the coupling, proposes the counter-intuitive asymmetric structure, and reaches J ~ 16.9 +/- 0.2 from any start; refining it with a classical optimizer attains the smooth global optimum (J ~ 12.0, 10/10 vs. 0/10), which even applies a non-obvious negative integral correction decentralized tuning cannot. A global optimizer (differential evolution) also reaches this optimum, so the LLM is not the only route; its advantage is sample efficiency and interpretability: a usable controller in 18 evaluations (where the global optimizer is worse than open loop) plus a stated rationale. This edge grows with dimension, reaching ~6x fewer evaluations on a 3x3 plant. The behaviour generalizes across four open models, and on a benign plant the LLM offers no advantage, sharpening the boundary. We contribute a reproducible benchmark delimiting when open LLMs help in control tuning: not as optimizers, but as a sample-efficient, interpretable structural prior.

</details>


### [296] [Superficial Beliefs in LLM Decision-Making](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11016)
*Gabriel Freedman,Francesca Toni*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 大语言模型的决策行为具有系统性的内部结构，但模型生成的理由往往无法准确反映其真实的决策逻辑，反映了模型对自身决策过程仅具备“肤浅的信念”。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探讨大语言模型在进行二元选择时，其输出的理由是真实的决策依据，还是仅仅对决策逻辑的伪装或模仿？即模型是否具有系统性的底层决策结构，以及模型对自身决策过程的自我意识程度如何。

Method: 研究者构建了合成的二元决策环境（模型需在由多个分级属性定义的选项中进行选择），通过行为建模拟合模型的决策模式，并将其与模型自述的理由以及基于评分的判定结果进行对比分析，同时进行了提示词顺序、采样干扰及结构化剔除等鲁棒性测试。

Result: 研究发现，大语言模型的决策行为具有高度的规律性和可预测性，表现出对特定属性的概率性偏好；然而，模型自述的决策理由往往无法准确对应其实际的决策驱动因素，这种“行为与解释不一致”的现象在多种实验条件下均保持稳定。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了大语言模型决策中的“肤浅信念”（superficial belief）概念：模型表现出系统性的决策逻辑，能够基于属性特征进行预测，但其生成的解释与实际驱动决策的底层逻辑之间存在显著的“认知鸿沟”，即模型缺乏对自身决策过程的准确反思能力。

Abstract: We ask whether large language models (LLMs) merely imitate rationales when choosing between two options, or whether their choices reflect a systematic underlying decision structure. Using synthetic binary decision settings in which models choose between profiles defined by graded attributes, we compare the attribute a model says mattered most with the attribute that best explains its choice under a behavioural model fit to prior decisions. The behavioural model predicts held-out choices well, showing that model behaviour is systematically related to the visible attributes rather than being random. However, direct self-reports and a separate score-based judge recover the behaviourally inferred driver only partially. The resulting picture is neither one of arbitrary behaviour nor one of fully articulated belief - outputs are structured enough to support prediction, but explicit reasons track the recovered driver only imperfectly. This qualitative pattern persists across prompt-order and sampling perturbations, alternative behavioural models, targeted occlusion analyses, and structurally varied decision settings. We interpret this as evidence for ``superficial belief'' in LLM decision-making: models behave as if guided by probabilistic local priorities over attributes, while having only limited verbal access to the attributes that drive their decisions.

</details>

Abstract: Recent years have witnessed the rapid evolution of AI agents toward handling increasingly complex, real-world tasks. However, existing benchmarks rarely evaluate whether agents can operate graphical user interfaces to complete long-horizon, high-value professional workflows across diverse domains. Current GUI benchmarks still predominantly focus on general-purpose software, relatively simple applications, and short-horizon tasks, leaving it largely unknown whether modern agents can follow user instructions to autonomously operate domain-specific professional software and accomplish economically valuable work in an end-to-end manner. To bridge this gap, we introduce Workflow-GYM, a benchmark for long-horizon GUI tasks centered on professional domains and specialized software environments. Through extensive experiments on state-of-the-art models, we find that even the strongest models achieve only slightly above 30% success rates, highlighting that professional long-horizon GUI workflows remain highly challenging for current GUI agents. Further analysis reveals that current agents struggle to maintain long-horizon workflow consistency, frequently exhibiting workflow stage omission, error propagation, objective drift, and insufficient understanding of professional software environments. Our findings provide important insights into the limitations of current agent systems and suggest key directions for the next generation of GUI-agent research.

### [298] [What Fits (Into Few Tokens) Doesn't Overfit: Compression and Generalization in ML Research Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11045)
*Martin Andres Bertran,Aaron Roth,Zhiwei Steven Wu*

TL;DR: 本研究通过对机器学习策略进行信息压缩实验，揭示了成功的AI开发策略具有高度可压缩性，这解释了为何基准驱动的机器学习在实践中不易产生过拟合。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解释为什么机器学习在重复使用留存基准测试时，实际发生的过拟合现象却远少于理论预期。作者提出了一个吸引人的假说：成功的机器学习策略是高度可压缩的。

Method: 研究者通过构建LLM驱动的研究智能体，设计了两种互补的信息瓶颈测试方法：1. 输出压缩：测试智能体在仅给定极短提示词和训练数据的情况下，是否能复现高表现模型；2. 输入压缩：测试仅给予“是否优于当前最优”的单位二进制反馈时，智能体能否找到高表现模型。此外，通过诱导过拟合进行反向验证以确保方法论的有效性。

Result: 在横跨表格分类、视觉、语言建模、扩散模型和奖励建模等8个数据集的实验中，作者发现信息瓶颈对模型性能影响微乎其微；短提示词和高压缩反馈足以寻找到或复现高表现模型。而在人为诱导过拟合的对照组中，短提示词无法有效复现结果。

Conclusion: 研究结果有力支持了“描述长度”假设，即基准驱动的机器学习中之所以很少出现过拟合，是因为成功的模型策略在策略空间中占据了低复杂度的区域。短描述（短提示词）即足以捕捉这些高表现的策略。

Abstract: Reusing a held-out benchmark adaptively should, in principle, invite overfitting. Yet benchmark-driven machine learning (ML) has produced surprisingly little overfitting in practice. An attractive hypothesis is that successful ML strategies are highly compressible. We study this in the setting of LLM-driven research agents, where the hypothesis becomes directly testable via two complementary information bottlenecks. In \emph{output compression}, an exploration agent adaptively searches for high-performance models using a validation set, and we test whether a fresh ``reproducer agent'' can reproduce its performance given only an extremely short prompt and the training data. In \emph{input compression}, the explorer receives only one-bit feedback indicating whether each submitted model improves on the running best. Across 8 datasets spanning tabular classification, vision, language modeling, diffusion modeling, and reward modeling, we find that these bottlenecks have little effect on performance: short prompts and compressible feedback are sufficient to reproduce and find high-performance models. The hypothesis is falsifiable: when we deliberately induce validation-set overfitting, the results fail to reproduce with short prompts. Taken together, our results support a description-length explanation for the lack of overfitting in benchmark-driven ML: successful strategies occupy a low-complexity region of strategy space.

</details>


### [299] [CIAware-Bench: Benchmarking Control Intervention Awareness Across Frontier LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11063)
*Joachim Schaeffer,Thomas Jiralerspong,Alexander Panfilov,Guillaume Lajoie,Jonas Geiping,Yoshua Bengio,Roland S. Zimmermann*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了CIAware-Bench基准测试，用于评估AI模型识别并规避控制干预的能力。研究发现模型普遍具备一定的CI感知力，且能通过识别特定风格特征来探测干预，这对设计更安全的AI监控协议提出了挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI系统常通过可信模型监控并干预不受信任模型的行为。然而，如果模型能够意识到这些干预，它可能推断出监控器的属性并进化出规避策略，从而导致控制机制失效。目前缺乏量化这种“控制干预感知能力”的工具。

Method: 构建了名为CIAware-Bench的基准测试，涵盖论文写作、代码生成（BigCodeBench）、Bash脚本和SHADE-Arena四个领域。通过改变轨迹水印、辅助任务和控制协议等变量，测试模型区分自身原始轨迹与经受控制干预后的轨迹的能力，并对11个前沿模型进行了实证评估。

Result: 在默认设置下，模型展现出低到中等的CI感知能力（最高准确率0.87，随机为0.5），不同任务和模型组合间的感知差异巨大。跨模型家族的检测通常更容易，暗示模型倾向于利用提供商特有的训练风格或后训练差异来识别干预。

Conclusion: 控制干预（CI）感知并非模型固有的静态属性，而是随任务场景和模型交互动态变化的。研究表明，现有的防御性控制协议存在被模型规避的风险，因此在部署AI控制方案时，必须针对具体模型和场景进行持续的CI感知评估，以设计更隐蔽、更有效的控制机制。

Abstract: AI control protocols oversee untrusted models by monitoring their actions and modifying potentially unsafe steps, often using a trusted model. This partially tampers with the untrusted model's trajectory. If the trusted model detects such an intervention, it may infer properties of the monitor and adapt to evade control. We introduce \textbf{CIAware-Bench}, a benchmark for measuring \textbf{c}ontrol \textbf{i}ntervention (CI) awareness across frontier models. CIAware-Bench tests whether models can distinguish their own trajectories from those modified by a control intervention. The benchmark is comprised of a suite of four task domains (essay writing, BigCodeBench, Bash Arena, and SHADE-Arena), while varying trajectory watermarking, side-task presence, and the control protocol. Evaluating eleven frontier models, we find low to moderate CI awareness under default settings (up to 0.87; random chance balanced binary classification accuracy is 0.5) with substantial variation across task domains and model pairs. Detection is generally easier across model families, suggesting that models exploit provider-specific differences in style or post-training. Overall, CI awareness is not a fixed model-level property, and should be measured for each new model release and deployment scenario. We release CIAware-Bench to track CI awareness and inform control protocols whose interventions are harder to detect.

</details>


### [300] [A History-Aware Visually Grounded Critic for Computer Use Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11078)
*Jaewoo Lee,Zaid Khan,Archiki Prasad,Justin Chih-Yao Chen,Supriyo Chakraborty,Kartik Balasubramaniam,Sambit Sahu,Elias Stengel-Eskin,Hyunji Lee,Mohit Bansal*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: HiViG是一个针对计算机使用智能体（CUA）的测试时评估框架，通过历史感知抽象与视觉接地批判，显著提升了智能体在复杂GUI环境下的长序列任务执行成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的计算机使用智能体（CUA）测试时评估方法存在两大局限：一是过于关注短视的决策循环，容易忽视任务全局；二是缺乏足够的视觉接地能力，无法有效识别针对UI元素的错误操作。

Method: 提出了一种名为HiViG的测试时评估框架，包含：1. 宏观动作历史模块，用于将历史交互抽象为紧凑记录，解决长序列规划短视问题；2. 视觉接地批判模块，通过将原始执行坐标与实时屏幕截图进行比对，在执行前过滤错误操作。该框架通过多模态批判模型进行训练，并集成于智能体的决策循环中。

Result: 在Web、移动端和桌面端的各项基准测试中，HiViG均表现优于现有的标量和语言批判模型。在Qwen3-VL-32B模型上平均成功率提升了5.8%，在Gemini-3-Flash模型上提升了9.0%，并表现出强大的跨平台泛化能力。消融实验证明了历史感知和视觉接地组件对于长序列GUI任务的至关重要性。

Conclusion: HiViG通过历史感知和视觉接地技术，有效克服了当前计算机使用智能体在长序列任务中的规划短视和执行错误问题，证实了该框架在复杂GUI环境中提升智能体决策能力的有效性和普适性。

Abstract: Various test-time interventions for Computer Use Agents (CUAs), including critic models, have been developed to improve performance through pre-execution action evaluation in complex Graphical User Interface (GUI) environments. However, existing critics suffer from two key limitations: they (1) focus primarily on short-sighted decision loops (e.g., forgetting earlier actions) and (2) lack the visual grounding needed to detect flawed actions (e.g., clicking wrong UI elements). To address these, we introduce HiViG, a History-aware Visually Grounded test-time framework, built around a multimodal critic trained on real GUI trajectories to abstract past interactions into a compact record and to evaluate actions with visual grounding. At test time, HiViG integrates the critic into the policy decision loop to provide macro-action history, which summarizes the policy's completed achievements, and visually grounded critique, which verifies raw execution coordinates against the current screenshot to intercept errors before execution. Across web, mobile, and desktop benchmarks, HiViG consistently outperforms existing scalar and verbal critics, improving average success rates over the strongest baseline by 5.8% for Qwen3-VL-32B and 9.0% for Gemini-3-Flash, and demonstrates strong cross-platform generalization. Ablations show that macro-action history mitigates short-sighted planning and visually grounded critique reduces execution errors, with both components being critical for test-time scaling in long-horizon GUI tasks.

</details>


### [301] [Monte Carlo Pass Search: Using Trajectory Generation for 3D Counterfactual Pass Evaluation in Football](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11120)
*Andrew Kang,Priya Narasimhan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了蒙特卡洛传球搜索（MCPS）框架，结合足球价值评估、轨迹模拟与反事实采样，利用自动驾驶领域的自回归轨迹生成技术，实现了对足球传球质量的分布感知评估与归因分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的足球传球评估往往局限于单一的统计指标或简单的轨迹预测，缺乏对传球执行变体（如不同的脚法或路径）及其潜在价值分布的深度评估。研究者旨在通过建立一个类似蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）的评估框架，利用高保真追踪数据，实现对传球决策和执行效果的更精准、更具解释性的量化分析。

Method: 本研究提出了一种名为“蒙特卡洛传球搜索”（MCPS）的方法。该方法整合了三个核心组件：1）价值模型（评估控球价值）；2）世界模型（基于SMART架构的离散标记自回归轨迹生成器，用于预测多智能体运动及球的交互）；3）策略模型（对传球动作进行反事实采样与变体模拟）。通过对实际传球进行多次模拟回放，并结合均值和百分位数两种评分指标，对传球的质量进行分布感知归因。

Result: 在德甲联赛的高保真追踪数据集上进行测试，MCPS方法表现优异。实验结果显示，所采用的基于SMART架构的轨迹生成器在“前20次预测”（best-of-20）准确度上显著优于现有基准模型，且能够有效支持假设性的传球后果模拟，从而生成可靠的传球价值分布。

Conclusion: 该研究通过蒙特卡洛传球搜索（MCPS）框架，成功地将足球传球评估转化为一种基于模拟的决策问题。该方法不仅能够准确评估传球表现，还能通过分布感知归因提供比传统单一指标更细致的分析，证明了从自动驾驶领域迁移轨迹生成技术（SMART）到足球运动建模的可行性和有效性。

Abstract: We recast pass evaluation in football (soccer) as a Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS)-like evaluation problem whose components mostly exist in the literature under different names: a value model (possession value), a world model (multi-agent trajectories with ball interactions), and a policy over counterfactual actions (sampling pass variants with noise). Building on the first public high-fidelity tracking dataset with 3D ball trajectories from the Bundesliga, we introduce Monte Carlo Pass Search (MCPS), which infers kick parameters for each observed pass, samples execution variants and option variants, rolls each candidate forward with a ball-conditioned world model until the next ball interaction, and scores outcomes with a learned value model to obtain a distribution over gained value. This distribution enables distribution-aware attribution with two complementary execution-surplus scores used for analysis and ranking: mean-based and percentile-based scores. To make the world model sample-efficient under limited public data, we adapt a discrete-token, autoregressive trajectory generator from autonomous driving (SMART) and show it yields strong best-of-20 forecasting accuracy compared to baselines, while supporting fully hypothetical rollouts for downstream evaluation. We have released model checkpoints and code.

</details>


### [302] [ABC-Bench: An Agentic Bio-Capabilities Benchmark for Biosecurity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11150)
*Andrew Bo Liu,Samira Nedungadi,Bryce Cai,Alex Kleinman,Harmon Bhasin,Seth Donoughe*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出了 ABC-Bench，这是一个衡量大语言模型在生物安全相关任务中能力的新基准，实验证明 AI 智能体已能有效执行包括自动化实验在内的复杂生物工程任务，表现甚至超过了人类专家，这引发了对生物安全监管的迫切需求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者开发了名为“ABC-Bench”的基准测试套件，专门评估智能体在生物安全相关任务中的能力。测试涵盖了良性和双重用途任务，包括：1) 编写操作液体处理机器人的代码；2) 设计用于体外组装的 DNA 片段；3) 规避 DNA 合成筛选。研究还进行了湿实验验证，利用 OpenAI 的 o4-mini-high 模型生成的脚本在 OpenTrons 机器人上成功组装了目标 DNA。

Result: 测试结果显示，所有受测的 LLM 智能体在三项任务上的表现均超过了人类专家基准的中位数。模型在依赖现有文献和成熟协议的任务中表现优异，但在需要创新生物信息学推理的任务上相对较弱。此外，湿实验验证确认了 AI 生成的脚本能够成功指挥实验硬件完成 DNA 组装。

Conclusion: 随着大语言模型代理在生物学任务中表现出超越人类专家的能力，其在生物安全领域的风险日益凸显。ABC-Bench 提供了一个关键的评估框架，证明了当前先进 AI 模型已具备执行复杂生物工程任务的潜力，亟需针对这些代理系统的生物安全监管和防御机制。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are rapidly acquiring capabilities relevant to biological research, from literature synthesis to interpretation of experimental data. These emerging AI capabilities offer new opportunities for scientific discovery and biomedical advances, but they also shift the landscape of biosecurity risks. To address this, we introduce the Agentic Bio-Capabilities Benchmark (ABC-Bench), a suite of tasks to measure agentic biosecurity-relevant capabilities. ABC-Bench evaluates LLM agents on both benign and dual-use biology tasks: writing code to operate liquid handling robots, designing DNA fragments for in vitro assembly, and evading DNA synthesis screening. These tasks require a combination of biology and software expertise. All tested LLM agents outperformed the median expert human baseliner on all three tasks. Agents performed highly on tasks drawing on published knowledge and well-documented protocols, and more weakly on a task requiring novel bioinformatics reasoning. In three wet-lab validation experiments, we found that OpenAI's o4-mini-high produced scripts that, when run on an OpenTrons liquid handling robot, successfully assembled DNA with expected sequences.

### [303] [ReasonAlloc: Hierarchical Decoding-Time KV Cache Budget Allocation for Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11164)
*Wenhao Liu,Hao Shi,Yunhe Li,Weizhi Fei,Xiangyuan Wang,Mengzhe Ruan,Hanxu Hou,Peisong Wang,Linqi Song,Shuang Qiu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ReasonAlloc 是一种无需训练的 KV Cache 压缩框架，通过离线层级预分配（捕获“推理波”）与在线头级动态分配相结合，解决了长思维链推理中的显存瓶颈，实现了在低资源消耗下的高性能推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大模型长思维链（Long CoT）推理过程中，KV Cache 的急剧增长导致严重的推理瓶颈。现有的压缩方法多采用均匀分配预算或仅针对预填充阶段设计，忽略了自回归推理过程中不同步骤对上下文需求的动态变化。

Method: ReasonAlloc 提出了“层次化预算分配”策略：1. 离线层级预分配：利用“推理波（Reasoning Wave）”模式，针对不同层级的架构需求分配预算；2. 在线头级动态分配：在解码过程中根据 Token 的实时效用，动态地将 KV Cache 资源重新分配给信息量更丰富的注意力头。该方法可与现有的 Token 剔除策略无缝集成。

Result: 在 MATH-500 和 AIME 2024 等数学推理基准测试上，使用 DeepSeek-R1-Distill 等模型进行验证，结果显示 ReasonAlloc 在小预算（128-512 Tokens）下优于 R-KV、SnapKV 和 Pyramid-RKV 等现有方法，且推理开销极低。

Conclusion: ReasonAlloc 提供了一种高效的、无需训练的 KV Cache 压缩框架，通过层次化的预算分配策略，成功缓解了长思维链推理带来的显存瓶颈，在保持模型推理性能的同时，显著提升了资源受限场景下的解码效率。

Abstract: Long chain-of-thought (CoT) trajectories in large language model (LLM) reasoning cause severe inference bottlenecks due to rapid key-value (KV) cache growth. Current decoding-time compression methods mitigate this issue via token eviction, but typically assume a uniform budget distribution across all layers and heads. In contrast, existing non-uniform budget allocation methods are predominantly designed for the static prompt prefill phase, and they do not capture the stepwise context demands of autoregressive reasoning. To bridge this gap, we propose ReasonAlloc, a training-free framework that recasts decoding-time KV compression as a hierarchical budget allocation problem. ReasonAlloc operates at two complementary levels: an offline layer-wise preallocation strategy captures an architecture-driven demand pattern which we call ``\textit{Reasoning Wave}'', while an online head-wise strategy reallocates resources during decoding to information-rich heads based on real-time utility. Evaluations on mathematical reasoning benchmarks (MATH-500, AIME~2024) using DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Llama-8B, DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-14B, and AceReason-14B show that ReasonAlloc outperforms uniform-budget R-KV, SnapKV, and Pyramid-RKV (a baseline enforcing a static, monotonically decreasing layer budget), with the largest gains at small budgets (128-512 tokens). ReasonAlloc is plug-and-play with existing token-eviction policies and introduces negligible inference-time overhead.

</details>


### [304] [The Role of Feedback Alignment in Self-Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11173)
*Semih Kara,Oğuzhan Ersoy*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了自我蒸馏中上下文反馈的设计，提出通过与模型推理轨迹对齐的“步骤化评论”进行蒸馏，显著优于传统的二进制奖励或参考答案对照，证明了反馈与推理过程结构化对齐的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自我蒸馏通过利用额外的上下文（如反馈）来提升语言模型表现，但现有的研究主要关注蒸馏过程本身，对于“反馈上下文应如何设计”这一关键问题缺乏探索。研究者希望通过优化反馈内容，提升模型在脱离额外上下文时的推理能力。

Method: 研究了自我蒸馏中的上下文设计问题，通过冻结的评论者（critic）生成的反馈对求解器进行训练，并对比了三种上下文设计方案：(i) 二进制奖励（GRPO）；(ii) 参考答案；(iii) 与求解器推理轨迹对齐的“步骤对齐评论”（step-by-step critique）。

Result: 实验表明，步骤对齐评论效果最佳，在 Avg@12 指标上比 GRPO 高出 16.11 分，比参考答案条件下的自我蒸馏高出 5.27 分。分析显示，这种方法能精准定位推理失误，避免了参考答案法中因推导路径差异而产生的误导性压力。

Conclusion: 结构化对齐（即反馈与求解器推理过程的对齐）是提升自我蒸馏效果的关键。与传统的二进制奖励或全解对照相比，针对推理失败步骤进行细粒度指导的“步骤对齐评论”能更有效地引导模型学习，同时避免破坏模型已掌握的正确推理逻辑。

Abstract: Conditioning a language model on additional context, such as feedback on a previous attempt, typically improves its response. Self-distillation trains the model to retain this improvement when the context is not present. The method works by matching the model's output distribution under two settings: a student that sees only the question, and a self-teacher that also sees the context. What the model learns therefore depends on what context the self-teacher receives, yet the design of this context remains largely unexplored.
  We study context design for self-distillation by training a solver on feedback from a frozen critic. We compare three conditions: (i) a binary reward (GRPO), (ii) the reference solution, and (iii) a step-by-step critique aligned to the solver's reasoning trace.
  Step-aligned critique yields the largest gains, outperforming GRPO by 16.11 points and reference-solution-conditioned self-distillation by 5.27 points (Avg@12). Per-token advantage analysis reveals why: step-aligned feedback targets only the tokens where reasoning fails, leaving correct behavior intact. Conditioning on the reference solution, by contrast, pressures the model to change its behavior at every token (even correct steps) because an alternative derivation inevitably differs in phrasing and approach. This suggests that structural alignment between feedback and the solver's reasoning is a key driver of self-distillation effectiveness.

</details>

### [305] [Mult-DPO: Multinomial Direct Preference Optimization for Recommender Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10078)
*Yaochen Zhu,Harald Steck,James McInerney,Aditya Sinha,Yinhan He,Nathan Kallus,Jundong Li*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对推荐系统中常见的集合偏好数据，本文提出了 Mult-DPO 算法，通过多项式代理似然函数解决了传统 DPO 在处理多个候选集时计算复杂的问题，实现了高效的大模型推荐对齐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的直接偏好优化（DPO）基于配对偏好，而推荐系统中常见的用户反馈通常是集合偏好（即多个正样本对比多个负样本）。将基础的 Plackett-Luce 奖励模型应用于此类数据存在组合爆炸的计算难题，因此需要一种更高效的对齐策略。

Method: 提出了一种名为 Mult-DPO 的新型优化目标。该方法利用多项式代理似然（multinomial surrogate likelihood）取代了 Plackett-Luce 模型中复杂的组合边际化计算，构建了一个可处理集合偏好数据的闭式（closed-form）DPO 目标函数，并证明了该目标是边际化 PL DPO 损失的一个易于处理的上界。

Result: 实验证明，Mult-DPO 在处理集合偏好数据时具有良好的计算性能，其损失函数是原问题的有效上界。研究还通过理论分析给出了该上界紧致性的条件，并将其扩展到了多级偏好场景，展现了在推荐系统中的实用价值。

Conclusion: Mult-DPO 为大语言模型推荐系统提供了一种有效且计算高效的偏好对齐框架，克服了传统配对偏好算法在处理集合偏好数据时的局限性，并为多层级偏好学习提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: Direct preference optimization (DPO) is a simple and effective alignment strategy for large language models (LLMs) based on pairwise preferences. In recommender systems, however, user feedback is rarely pairwise. For a given context, e.g., a user, a session, or a conversation, we typically observe set-wise preferences with multiple positive items, where every positive item should outrank every unobserved or explicitly negative item, with no prescribed order among the positives or the negatives themselves. A natural generalization is to use the Plackett-Luce (PL) reward model, which extends the Bradley-Terry reward model underlying vanilla DPO from pairwise preferences to full rankings of candidates. However, we show that adapting the PL model to set-wise preferences requires marginalizing over all positive orderings, where the resulting expression is combinatorial in complexity. To address this fundamental challenge, we propose Mult-DPO, a novel DPO objective with a tractable multinomial surrogate likelihood over set-wise preference events for the user-preference alignment of LLM-based recommender systems. The multinomial construction is not itself a ranking distribution, but it is defined on the same reward-induced weight space and admits a closed-form DPO-style objective, enabling direct alignment of LLMs with multiple candidates through a classification-style objective. In addition, we prove that the multinomial DPO loss is a tractable upper bound on the marginalized PL DPO loss when optimizing against the set-wise preference data. We further characterize the tightness of this bound in terms of the relative total weight of positives versus negatives, which provides insights into tightening the bound with richer or harder negatives. Finally, we extend Mult-DPO to the alignment of LLMs with multiple preference levels. Code is available at https://github.com/yaochenzhu/Mult_DPO

</details>


### [306] [MetaPlate: Counterfactual-Guided RAG-LLM Tool for Personalized Food Recommendation and Hyperglycemia Prevention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10120)
*Asiful Arefeen,Carol Johnston,Hassan Ghasemzadeh*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: MetaPlate是一个结合CGM数据、机器学习预测与LLM生成能力的个性化饮食辅助系统，通过反事实优化与约束生成技术，为用户提供切实可行且能有效平稳餐后血糖的饮食建议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的饮食指导多为静态且缺乏个性化，难以有效控制餐后高血糖。当前的血糖预测模型虽能预知血糖变化，但缺乏可落地的行动建议，且现有的推荐系统往往忽略用户真实需求或过于复杂，导致依从性差。因此，研究旨在开发一种能够提供实时、个性化且具备临床可行性饮食建议的智能系统。

Method: MetaPlate是一个上下文感知的决策支持框架，其核心流程包括：1) 利用连续血糖监测（CGM）和穿戴设备数据对个体进行建模；2) 使用机器学习模型预测餐后血糖反应；3) 采用反事实优化（CF Optimization）模块调整餐食宏量营养素构成，以确保血糖处于安全范围；4) 引入基于LLM的检索增强生成（RAG）层，在USDA数据库约束下，将优化后的建议转化为可读的饮食方案。

Result: 通过注册营养师参与的结构化评估，MetaPlate生成的建议在真实性、分量合理性以及用户采纳可能性方面均有显著提升。实验证实，通过引入领域知识约束，系统成功克服了LLM在饮食推荐中常出现的“幻觉”和临床不可行问题，生成了更具实用价值的个性化饮食方案。

Conclusion: MetaPlate展示了结合领域知识、结构化约束与大型语言模型（LLM）的决策支持系统在个性化饮食管理中的巨大潜力。通过引入反事实解释与检索增强生成（RAG），该框架能够生成临床上可行且符合语境的建议，为实时个性化饮食干预提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Postprandial hyperglycemia is a key risk factor for metabolic disorders; however, existing dietary guidance is often static, impractical, and insufficiently personalized, providing recommendations that are difficult to follow or not impactful. While recent advances leverage continuous glucose monitoring (CGM) and machine learning to predict glycemic responses, these approaches are largely predictive and lack actionable guidance. Moreover, recommendation systems are often misaligned with user goals and require extensive input. We present MetaPlate, a counterfactual explanation (CF) guided, context-aware decision-support framework that generates personalized meal recommendations to mitigate postprandial glucose excursions in healthy adults. MetaPlate integrates multimodal data, including CGM readings, wearable-derived physiological signals, and user-provided meal inputs from $25$ individuals to model pre-meal context. A machine learning model predicts glucose response, while a CF optimization module adjusts meal composition modifying macronutrient amounts to maintain glucose levels within a target range ($\leq 140$ mg/dL). An LLM-based retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) layer enhances interpretability by producing human-readable recommendations using constrained search of the USDA food database. We evaluate MetaPlate via a structured expert-in-the-loop assessment with registered dietitians (RDs), comparing performance before and after prompt refinement. Results show improvements in meal realism, portion suitability, and recommendation likelihood, with expert feedback indicating a shift from clinically implausible outputs to actionable, contextually appropriate recommendations. Our findings emphasize the importance of domain knowledge and structured constraints in LLM-driven systems and highlight the potential of MetaPlate as a real-time personalized dietary decision-support tool.

### [307] [$τ$-Rec: A Verifiable Benchmark for Agentic Recommender Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10156)
*Bharath Sivaram Narasimhan,Karthik R Narasimhan*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个名为τ-Rec的基准测试，旨在取代主观的“LLM-as-a-judge”评测，通过可验证的奖励机制和约束控制来评估代理式推荐系统的逻辑可靠性。实验揭示了当前顶尖模型在处理复杂推荐任务时性能表现远低于预期，存在明显的可靠性缺口。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了τ-Rec基准测试框架，核心包括：1. 基于结构化目录谓词的可验证奖励机制，消除主观性；2. 揭示标签启发（RTE）机制，用于精确控制任务约束在对话中的呈现方式；3. 采用pass^k可靠性指标，系统评估智能体在多轮交互中的推理一致性。

Result: 对五种模型家族的九种配置进行了测试，发现模型性能存在“可靠性悬崖”：顶级模型在pass^1指标下仅达到约57%的准确率，在pass^4指标下仅为约38%，显示出现有智能体在执行复杂推荐任务时存在严重的逻辑一致性缺陷。

Conclusion: 当前主流大语言模型在代理式推荐任务中表现出显著的可靠性不足（可靠性悬崖），在多轮对话中处理复杂约束的能力远未达到部署要求。该研究强调了开发更具逻辑严密性和可验证性的评测框架的必要性。

Abstract: As recommender systems transition toward agentic, multi-turn conversational interfaces, evaluation paradigms have struggled to keep pace. Current benchmarks often rely on "LLM-as-a-judge" evaluations, which introduce subjectivity, high costs and inconsistency. We present $τ$-Rec, a benchmark for agentic recommender systems that replaces subjective evaluation with verifiable rewards and a reveal-tagged elicitation (RTE) mechanism that controls how task constraints surface during dialogue. By testing agents against structured catalog predicates and employing a pass^k reliability metric, $τ$-Rec provides a systematic test for consistent reasoning. Our evaluation of nine configurations across five model families -- GPT-5.4, Claude Sonnet 4.6, Gemini 2.5 Flash, DeepSeek V4 Flash, Qwen3-32B and GPT-5 mini -- reveals a steep reliability cliff, where even the best model achieves only ~57% at pass^1 and ~38% at pass^4, highlighting a critical gap in current conversational agent deployment. All code and data are publicly available at https://github.com/nbharaths/tau-rec.

Although large language models (LLMs) possess powerful semantic understanding and reasoning capabilities, their millisecond-level inference latency makes direct application in online recommendation systems difficult. To address these issues, this paper introduces AIR (Atomic Intent Reasoning), an LLM-driven cross-domain recommendation framework designed for industrial-grade deployment. By migrating LLM inference to the offline phase and dynamically constructing user intent representations through efficient retrieval and composition during online operations, it achieves approximately 400* inference acceleration while maintaining semantic consistency. ### [309] [SIDInspector: A Mapping-First Diagnostic Resource for Semantic-ID Tokenizers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10375)
*Jiandong Ding,Heng Chang,Huijie Qin,Tianying Liu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 该论文提出了诊断工具SID-Diag，用于在生成式推荐系统训练前评估语义ID分词器的质量，通过发现编码映射中的缺陷（如高别名率）来优化推荐性能，并明确了地址空间评估的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在生成式推荐系统中，语义ID（Semantic-ID）分词器（Tokenizer）常被作为独立工件重用。然而，这些编码映射缺乏通用的检查接口，导致常见的缺陷（如别名、尾部压缩、覆盖缺失等）往往要在下游训练完成后才能发现，从而造成资源浪费和性能瓶颈。

Method: 作者提出了一个名为SID-Diag的诊断工具。该工具定义了一个统一的适配器契约，用于集成物品映射、元数据、交互记录及生成器追踪。SID-Diag通过对利用率、别名率、邻域对齐、流行度分配和结构成本等维度进行映射级探测，并在下游模型训练前提供可检查的制品配置文件。

Result: 实验对比了四种不同的Tokenizer工件。结果显示，某些流行的编码方法（如GRID-style）存在高达97.7%的全码别名率，而其他方法（如ReSID/GAOQ）则无别名。此外，研究发现分类前缀控制在协同对齐方面表现最佳，优于所学习的导出行，这表明当前的语义ID设计在地址意义和前缀对齐方面仍有显著提升空间。

Conclusion: 研究表明，语义ID（Semantic-ID）的编码映射质量直接影响生成式推荐的效果。通过诊断工具SID-Diag，作者揭示了现有Tokenizers存在的严重问题（如别名、覆盖率不足等），并强调地址空间的可寻址性和前缀的语义意义应被作为独立的评估维度，以便在下游训练前及时识别潜在瓶颈。

Abstract: Semantic-ID (\sid) tokenizers are increasingly reused as standalone artifacts in generative recommendation: an exported item-to-code mapping becomes the address space that a later sequence generator must use. These mappings rarely come with a common inspection interface, so coverage gaps, full-code aliasing, behaviorally weak prefixes, tail compression, and prefix fan-out are often found only after downstream training. We present \tool, a mapping-first diagnostic resource for \sid tokenizer artifacts. \tool defines a small adapter contract over item mappings, metadata, interactions, and optional generator traces; validates the contract; and reports mapping-level probes for utilization, aliasing, neighborhood alignment, popularity allocation, and structural cost, with hooks for temporal churn and generator traces.
  \tool reports inspectable artifact profiles before downstream leaderboard scores. The released resource covers four tokenizer artifact lines: a same-item GRID/RQ-KMeans-style and ReSID/GAOQ contrast on 23,742 Musical items, plus released LETTER and LC-Rec item-index artifacts. In the Musical contrast, the GRID-style feature-text export has 3,749 unique full codes and a 0.977 full-code aliasing rate, while ReSID/GAOQ is aliasing-free in its exported mapping. Yet the strongest prefix--co-occurrence alignment comes from a deterministic category-prefix control, not from either learned export row (0.447 versus 0.154 and 0.055--0.080), showing that addressability and behaviorally meaningful prefixes should be inspected separately. Cross-domain, fixed-reranker, and mechanism-probe checks support the same diagnostic direction: prefix alignment is a candidate-exposure signal, while final ranking quality remains a downstream model question.

### [310] [SkillResolve-Bench: Measuring and Resolving Same-Capability Ambiguity in Agent Skill Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10388)
*Jiandong Ding*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对智能体技能库检索中常见的“语义相似但执行风险不同”的问题，本论文提出了 SkillResolve-Bench 1.0 基准和 SkillResolve 方法，通过在检索中引入家族代表选择机制，在保证检索准确性的同时消除了因选取错误版本而带来的执行风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在智能体应用中，仅根据相关性检索技能存在风险。即便检索到了正确的技能类别，也可能选出具体的错误版本（如陈旧资源或错误流程的“高风险兄弟技能”），导致执行失败。作者旨在解决这一“同能力执行风险检索”难题。

Method: 作者提出了 SkillResolve-Bench 1.0 基准测试，并开发了 SkillResolve 方法。该方法核心步骤包括：解析候选技能家族、基于混淆负样本与合约配置线索评分查询条件效用，并在最终排序前执行“家族内代表选择”，确保所选技能的安全性与准确性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过在检索过程中引入“家庭内代表选择（representative selection）”机制，可以将单纯的语义匹配提升为更安全的程序化暴露，从而有效降低智能体执行风险，同时提升检索精度。

Abstract: Agent skill libraries are becoming routable software assets: a retrieved skill can contribute instructions, scripts, resource bindings, and execution assumptions to an agent. This makes skill retrieval more than broad relevance matching. A retriever can find the right capability family yet expose the wrong same-capability representative. We study this failure as same-capability execution-risk retrieval. Each query pairs a helpful skill with a query-specific risky sibling that shares the capability family but can lead execution toward a stale resource, missing precondition, or wrong procedure. We introduce SkillResolve-Bench 1.0, an auditable benchmark for this setting with 661 helpful/risky pairs, source-role and admission evidence, cue/leakage checks, query-disjoint splits, and a 7,982-candidate pool that includes 6,660 public SkillRet candidates. The benchmark reports helpful ranking together with harmful sibling rate (HSR@K), the top-K exposure of the risky sibling. We also provide SkillResolve, a reference method that resolves active candidate families, scores query-conditioned utility from confusable library negatives and contract-profile cues, and selects one representative from each family before the final top-K list. Under the released family relation, SkillResolve reaches Recall@3 0.766 and NDCG@3 0.699 while keeping HSR@3=0. It improves over SkillRouter by 0.112 Recall@3 and 0.165 NDCG@3 while reducing HSR@3 from 0.693 to 0. Without representative selection, HSR@3 rises to 0.236 under the same scorer, identifying within-family representative choice as the mechanism that turns capability retrieval into safer procedural exposure.
